Shanghai-Qingjiang Direct Telegraph Line 151

Installation Has Already Begun

Will Be Completed Soon

Wired telegrams sent from Shanghai to various places north of the Yangtze River have been forwarded by the Zhenjiang Telegraph Office. After reaching the Qingjiang Telegraph Office, they are gradually redistributed to various places. The process has been lengthy and frequent. It is now known that the Ministry of Communications, for the convenience of all sectors of society, has planned to install a direct telegraph line from Shanghai to Qingjiang. All materials have already been prepared, and construction began the other day. The construction of the telegraph line is expected to be fully completed by the end of this month or the beginning of next month. The telegraph machines adopted this time are the latest Western high-speed machines in the world. Once the assembly is complete, direct reporting can be scheduled regularly, without the need for forwarding by the Zhenjiang Telegraph Office.

A Large Gambling Den Cracked Down on Haichang Road 152

All Kinds of Gambling Equipment Were Present

Hundreds of Gamblers

The Gambling Boss Was a Police Officer

At 0:20 a.m. yesterday morning, the Public Security Bureau of the Fourth District of Zhabei, acting on a tip-off, learned that someone had set up a large gambling den inside the rickshaw company at No. 12 on a branch road of Haichang Road, complete with all kinds of gambling equipment such as rolling dice and pai gow. District Chief Lai, after receiving the report, immediately ordered Inspector Peng Wenwei to lead the police to the address. When they arrived at the rickshaw company, they found the iron gate tightly closed, making it impossible to enter. They had to shout outside, which was heard by the gamblers inside, and the order became extremely chaotic for a while. The gamblers scattered and fled in all directions. When the iron gate was opened, hundreds of gamblers rushed out. Because the police were too few in number, they could not stop them all. As a result, they only captured the owner, Bai Zhenggang (the rickshaw company boss), Yang Jinghua, the gambling boss who was skimming profits from the gambling (a police officer from the Fourth District Public Security Bureau), and twelve other gamblers, including Li Rushan, Bai Zhenrong, Zhao Shigen, Cao Jinji, Li Xiaosanzi, Yuan Defu, Dai Shihe, Gu Baoluan, Li Tingfang, and Xu Shaoqing. Among them was a member of the security team, who was immediately released. Several sets of gambling equipment were confiscated, such as pai gow, chips (used in place of gambling funds), as well as other paper receipts and red pills, and all were taken to the district office. Unexpectedly, after the owner, Bai Zhenggang, arrived at the district office, he dared to roar and curse loudly. After questioning by the interrogating officer, it was determined that Bai and others knew that their actions were illegal and dared to openly insult public officials, which was extremely unlawful. Therefore, it was ordered that they be sent to the Public Security Bureau for punishment.

Striving for Punctuality of Arrival Times

The Joint Transportation Office of the Ministry of Railways sent a letter yesterday to the administrations of the two lines, saying that the punctuality of the arrival times of the Shanghai-Beiping Joint Transportation Service is of great importance to the convenience of passengers and should be strived for. Xu Kaitai Embezzles Public Funds; Receives Suspended Sentence Because He Surrendered Himself 154

Xu Kaitai, from Ningbo, had been working as a treasurer at the Qutainbao Silver Shop at No. 500 Nanjing Road for many years. He was usually diligent in his duties. Later, because his younger brother, Kai Fu, embezzled more than a thousand gold coins at the Qinghua Silver Shop, Xu tried to repay the money out of brotherly affection. From then on, Xu felt financially strapped and thought of engaging in "biaojin" (speculative transactions) to make up for it, but he suffered losses repeatedly, amounting to more than ten thousand gold coins. He then embezzled 120 taels of silver from the funds under his control, worth 14,000 yuan. By the end of last year, Xu feared that the matter would be discovered and affect his guarantors, so he informed the manager, Yao Guiqing. Unexpectedly, the shop did not make things difficult for Xu and only negotiated with the guarantors. Xu had no choice but to surrender himself to the Old Gate Police Station on the 16th of the month, accompanied by a lawyer. The police station's lawyer, Li Zhishan, filed a public prosecution for embezzlement in the course of business. The First Special Court concluded the interrogation yesterday morning, with Qian Hongye, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, ascended to the First Criminal Tribunal and announced the judgment. The main text of the judgment was: Xu Kaitai is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for continuous embezzlement of property held in the course of business. The number of days of detention before the final judgment will be credited against the imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment, with a three-year suspended sentence.

Ministry of Communications Consolidates Errors in Place Names in Radio Transmissions and Receipts 155

All Transmissions Should Follow the English Names

And May Not Use Radio Call Signs to Replace Place Names

Yan Renxian, Director of the Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications, recently noticed that there were frequent errors in the place names of receiving and transmitting radio stations. In order to rectify this, he stipulated that the place names of receiving and transmitting stations should uniformly use English names to avoid confusion. Yesterday, he sent a special telegram to all radio stations in the city to comply, the original text of which is as follows: All radio stations are aware: It has been found that errors frequently occur in the place names of receiving and transmitting radio stations, and repeated inquiries not only delay the time but also miss opportunities. It is necessary to actively rectify this to emphasize the importance of business. Hereafter, when your station transmits telegrams to various places, the place names of the receiving and transmitting stations should be particularly careful to avoid errors in receiving and transmitting. All transmissions must be sent using the English names to avoid confusion. The use of radio call signs to replace place names is not allowed. The same procedure should be followed when communicating between receiving and transmitting branches and radio stations. I hope everyone will comply.

A Dead Child Revives, But Dies Again 156

A Short-Lived Ghost Is Still a Short-Lived Ghost

Liu Dingliang Has a Momentary Joy

Liu Dingliang, from Ningbo, started his business in laundry and dyeing. He opened four Liu Juchang laundry and dyeing shops in the Xiaodongmen and Puxi Laiyidu areas. His family was fairly well-off. However, Liu was approaching forty years old and still had Bo Dao's worries [i.e., he was childless]. His wife had given birth five or six times, but all the babies had died young. Liu was quite superstitious and suspected that they were

Haunted by Debt-Collecting Ghosts 157

Therefore, after the children died, he performed all sorts of laughable actions to prevent the debt-collecting ghosts from reincarnating. Last year, his wife became pregnant again, and by the end of the year, her abdomen was bulging. On the fourth day of the Lunar New Year, she went into labor and gave birth to a boy, who was very plump. Liu was extremely happy because the delivery date coincided with the day of welcoming the God of Wealth, and he treated the child as a treasure. Unexpectedly, the baby was still a short-lived ghost and died again on the eighth night. Liu was very angry and only suspected that it was a debt-collecting ghost reincarnated, so he used

Black Ash to Smear His Face 158

Believing that he would no longer reincarnate next time, he wrapped the body in a reed mat and, on the morning of the ninth (i.e., the day before yesterday), ordered a shop assistant to carry it to a public burial ground near Wu Jiatin and abandon it. In the afternoon, wild dogs gathered around the reed mat, seemingly wanting to fight for the child's corpse. This was seen by residents in the area, and kind-hearted people went to pull open the reed mat. They were shocked to see the child, and they were suspicious. Coincidentally, Zhan Qikang, a traditional Chinese medicine doctor from the Qingyuchang Pharmacy on Laiyibo Street, was returning by car from a medical consultation in the east end and passed by the area. He also curiously entered the crowd and saw that the child could still be saved, so he took him home, applied massage techniques, and administered medicine. The child was able to cry and revive. Zhan cherished the child because he was a boy and

Specially Hired a Wet Nurse 159

To breastfeed him. This miraculous event quickly caused a sensation in the neighborhood, and people flocked to see it. Liu's shop was not far away, and the news soon reached him. Liu was curious and went to Zhan's shop to see that it was indeed his own son who had died and come back to life. He was overjoyed for a moment and wanted to take him home, but Zhan refused. Liu then asked people to intercede with Zhan, willing to have the child temporarily fostered in Zhan's care, and would also prepare a plaque as a gift and publish an advertisement for seven days to thank him for saving his life. He would also replace the hired wet nurse's clothes with new ones as compensation. After the conditions were agreed upon, just as they were about to implement them, who knew that the child would die again yesterday from phlegm obstruction? So a comedy became an illusion.

Authorities of Five Provinces and Cities Solemnly Appoint Motor Vehicle Driving Examiners 160

And Establish Temporary Driver's License Issuance Regulations

In order to solemnly appoint motor vehicle driving examiners, the authorities of five provinces and cities—Zhejiang, Anhui, Nanjing, Shanghai—have established the standards for the appointment of motor vehicle driving examiners in five provinces and cities, as well as temporary driver's license issuance regulations. The original text is recorded below: (1) Each province and city shall appoint motor vehicle driving examiners who have a qualification of graduating from a technical school above the secondary level, or who have worked in a transportation agency for more than three years and have rich experience in motor vehicle mechanics and driving, in order to be qualified. (2) After the examiners of each province and city take office, the competent authority shall submit the examiner's resume and seal to the Transportation Committee of the Five Provinces and Cities for filing, and distribute the seal sample to the relevant agencies in other provinces and cities for reference. If there is a change, the procedures are the same. (3) If a driver examined by an examiner of each province and city causes an accident within six months due to unskilled technology, the examiner shall be subject to appropriate punishment. If there is evidence of favoritism or other malpractices, in addition to handling in accordance with the law, the Transportation Committee shall also send a letter to the relevant agencies in the five provinces and cities, and they shall not be re-employed. (4) If the agencies in each province and city handling the issuance of licenses have not established qualified examiners, they may first issue temporary licenses with the approval of the provincial and municipal competent authorities, restricting driving in designated areas. After the Transportation Committee or the competent authority dispatches personnel to re-examine and pass within three months, a unified license will be issued. The fee charged for the aforementioned temporary license shall be the same as that for the unified license, but no additional fee shall be charged for reissuing the unified license. (5) These measures shall be resolved by the Transportation Committee of the Five Provinces and Cities, and a letter shall be sent to the National Economic Commission for forwarding to the provincial and municipal governments for promulgation and implementation.

Inventor of Electric Essence, Lu Dongsheng, Adopts Qing Stone to Refine Electric Essence 167

Electric Essence Lamps Are Highly Economical

Yunnan Tycoon Invests Heavily in Joint Venture

Mr. Lu Dongsheng spent ten years of painstaking effort to invent a kind of electric essence, the effectiveness of which is extremely great. In addition to being used as fuel, it can also be used to manufacture fertilizer powder, alcohol, and other substances, which has aroused the extreme attention of the scientific community at home and abroad. Recently, he plans to use domestic green stone to refine electric essence, in order to lower prices. The details are as follows:

Qing Stone Refining 168

According to Mr. Lu, speaking to a reporter from the Dagong News Agency, electric essence has a wide range of uses. Most of what our country currently uses comes from Europe and the United States, and the annual loss is considerable. After careful research by yours truly, the green stone produced in Suzhou, Hangzhou, and other places in our country is indeed the best raw material for manufacturing electric essence. It is planned to raise funds to open a company within the year to engage in development and actively refine electric essence, in order to stop the leakage of money.

Light Testing 169

The electric essence lamps invented by Mr. Lu currently sold on the market include two types: hanging lamps and table lamps. The results of testing the light are: Type A, 25-candlepower table lamps, cost 15 "zhi" worth of electric essence and can burn for one hour. If the light is increased to 75 "zhi", it only costs one cent of silver. Every half hour, enough rice can be cooked for three people. Type B, 15-candlepower table lamps, cost 12 "zhi" and can burn for one hour. 150-candlepower hanging lamps cost only seven cents of silver per pound of electric essence and can be used for four and a half hours.

Enthusiastic Investment 170

It is understood that after inventing electric essence, Mr. Lu continued to invent a kind of electric essence lamp that uses electric essence to ignite, and established a Huaming Electric Essence Lamp Factory to actively manufacture various lamp styles and sell them in various places. Recently, in order to expand the scope, it is planned to increase capital. It is heard that Yunnan tycoon Mr. Wu Xingzai has already subscribed to 20,000 shares, and in recent days, subscribers and investors from this port and other ports have been quite enthusiastic.

To Be Implemented from the Fifth Phase

The fourth phase of the aviation lottery tickets issued by the Ministry of Finance is scheduled to be drawn publicly at Yiyuan on Yapei Road in the French Concession on March 2. Two Gambling Cases Separately Sentenced 179

Xie Guangming, the chief detective, Hang Bingquan, the deputy detective, and detectives Cai Zongyi, He Zongyu, and Xiao Yu from the French Concession police's gambling squad, learned that someone was gambling at pai gow inside the Dahua Hotel at No. 85 Yuqing Lane, No. 261 Xixinqiao Street, violating the ban. They rushed to the scene at 12:30 AM the night before. First, in room 26 on the second floor, they arrested the banker Qin Yonglin, gamblers Sheng Xiaodi, and 15 others, seizing a set of pai gow, a set of playing cards, three yuan in silver, and 124 copper coins. Then, in room 44 on the third floor, they arrested the banker Sun Wanzhi, gamblers Xu Taocheng, and 13 others, seizing a set of pai gow, a set of playing cards, eleven yuan in silver, thirty-three double-corner coins, and 144 copper coins. After the search, they determined that the hotel had allowed gambling, violating the regulations of the Public Concession's hotel industry. Therefore, they took the hotel owner and manager Yu Huasheng to the police station together. Yesterday, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, where the police lawyer filed separate charges. After questioning by Judge Qiu, he immediately announced the judgment in court. Sun Wanzhi was sentenced to one month of imprisonment, and the remaining bankers and gamblers were fined five yuan each. The gambling equipment and funds were confiscated. Yu Huasheng was fined 20 yuan as a warning for violating the regulations by allowing gambling. Each defendant was allowed bail pending appeal.

Ministry of Interior Promulgates Regulations for Red Cross Membership Recruitment 180

The Chinese Red Cross Society, by order of the Ministry of Interior, will begin recruiting members on March 1, and has issued various measures. The fees are as follows: Student membership, one yuan per person; Ordinary membership, ten yuan; Full membership, twenty-five yuan; Special membership, two hundred yuan; Honorary membership, one thousand yuan. Provincial governors, mayors, and county magistrates are automatically chairmen due to the presence of branch offices in their jurisdictions. The reward methods are as follows: those who achieve 100 points or more will be promoted to ordinary membership; 500 points or more, full membership; 1,000 points or more, special membership; 5,000 points or more, honorary membership; 10,000 points or more, honorary membership, and a recommendation will be submitted to the Ministry of Interior for commendation. Those who can construct all or part of a Red Cross society building, hospital, or school will have their names inscribed on stone tablets or cast in bronze statues for eternal remembrance. Branches and teams with a total score of 1,000 or more will be awarded a banner; 5,000 or more, a plaque; 10,000 or more, both a banner and a plaque; 50,000 or more, a recommendation will be submitted to the Ministry of Interior for commendation.

Zhu Xuefan was publicly elected as chairman, and Fang Rusheng as recorder.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Zhu Xuefan began by stating that there were two main issues for today's temporary representative meeting of labor unions: (1) the organizational issue of this association. It was previously reported that the Central People's Movement Committee ordered this association to change its name to the National Salvation Federation, which caused dissatisfaction among the labor unions, who requested the central government to confirm the organization of the General Labor Union. However, there is no satisfactory solution yet. (2) The National Labor Representatives have been designated by the government in the past, or by Central Committee members acting in their place, which violates the interests of the labor community. Therefore, this association advocates that the representatives for this year should be elected by the labor community in various regions. Regarding the above two points, this association has sent representatives to petition the central government and they have now returned to Shanghai. Therefore, we plan to report on the progress and discuss future steps.

Petition Progress: Next, the Beijing representative Shao Xubai reported on the petition progress, stating that this association had sent representatives to petition the central government in Beijing regarding the issue of recognition and the issue of National Labor Representatives. After arriving in Beijing, they went to the Central People's Movement Committee to visit Director Wang Luyi. However, because Wang was in Shanghai visiting the sick Yu Youren, they were not able to meet him. Secretary Yang Donglin met with them instead and replied that (1) the central government has decided to accept the proposed opinion on the selection of National Labor Representatives and will appoint those with sufficient experience and sound physical condition from the labor community. However, due to time constraints, it may be difficult to follow the proposal of automatic selection by various regions. (2) Regarding the organization of the General Labor Union, it is difficult for the central government to recognize it because it is not based on law. As for the revision of the Trade Union Law, he agreed to forward it to Chairman Wang for review. They then went to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to petition. Because Minister Chen had a meeting, they were received by Section Chief Bao Huaguo of the Labor Department, who gave a similar reply. The next day, they went to the Central Party Headquarters to petition, and were received by Secretary-General Ye Chucang. After the representatives submitted the document and expressed their opinions, he replied that regarding the National Labor Representatives, he would forward it to the People's Movement Committee. Regarding the General Labor Union, the central government cannot but recognize it in fact, but it is not convenient to recognize it by law. He agreed to provide assistance within the possible scope. Later, they met with Central Organization Minister Chen Lifu. Chen expressed a good impression of the past work of the General Labor Union and instructed the future direction of the labor movement. The representatives felt that their mission had been completed, so they immediately returned to Shanghai by car. In short, the results of this trip were quite satisfactory. Although the central committee members did not formally recognize the General Labor Union due to legal restrictions, they all deeply knew that this association was a powerful Shanghai worker collective, and were also able to deeply understand its past work. Long Peiyun then reported on the points instructed by Chen Lifu, hoping that the entire Shanghai labor community would work hard on (1) awakening national consciousness, (2) strengthening spiritual organization, and (3) intensifying production construction to revive China.

Discussion of Proposals: After the report, the following proposals were discussed and resolved: (1) Before the Trade Union Law is revised, should we strive again to fight for the central government on the issue of the General Labor Union? It was resolved to intensify organization and continue to strive. (2) Although the central government has recognized the selection of National Labor Representatives from the labor community, should we continue to petition for the implementation of self-selection? It was resolved that due to time constraints, we would wait for the next session to continue to strive. (3) Should various labor unions jointly issue a statement supporting Wang and Jiang's telegraphic advocacy? It was resolved to pass it.

Gambling Den Cracked Down in Huatong Warehouse 185

Inside the Taikoo Company's Pudong Huatong Warehouse, before the recovery of police power, large gambling dens were openly opened every year at the end of the lunar year, gathering crowds for gambling. Since the Public Security Bureau sent police to take over, such people have slightly restrained themselves in recent years. In November of the last lunar year, Ningbo people Hu Baoquan and others secretly set up a gambling venue in the warehouse, gathering for gambling all night, which has continued to this year and is on a large scale. Zhang, the district chief of the Third District, learned of this and secretly sent Officer Liu and Police Chief Guo and others to the warehouse to search and arrest. As expected, the gambling venue was cracked down, and the banker Hu Baoquan, gamblers Ying Zongfa, Hou Xingkang, Fu Yuanhe, Shi Wenfu, Zhang Yingqing, Chen Desheng, Zheng Zhongyi, Li Xianhua, Zhou Shaohua, Su Huichao, and 10 others were arrested on the spot, along with gambling equipment and funds, and were taken to the district for interrogation. It was found that this gambling den was cracked down for the first time in decades.

Gathering for Gambling in Vacant Space 186

At No. 43 Anping Street in the city, there is a vacant house owned by a Li family, with a rather large backyard. Recently, local ruffians have used the vacant house to set up a gambling den, widely recruiting gamblers, and claiming that the local authorities have been taken care of and there is no need to worry. Therefore, many people gather to gamble and profit from commissions. The den offers various gambling games such as mahjong, poker, and pai gow. There are often dozens of people gambling inside, and accomplices are assigned to take turns watching at various key points, with extreme vigilance. At 4:00 PM yesterday, the director of the Second Division of the First District, Liu Yunfang, acting on a tip from a secret agent, personally led officers Hu Qiuqiao and Zhang Panchi, police chiefs Li Fuyi and Zhang Weichuan, and police officers, all dressed as gamblers, to capture them separately. However, the gambling den had many exits, allowing many to escape. Li Wangshi, Yan Dinghai, Zhou Yinfu, Zhang Yanhai, Zhao Zigang, Zhang Erbao, Lei Fugen, Yang Yongjin, Zhu Peifang, Wu Shaozhi, Teng Xiaoxing, Chen Jinsheng, Yu Sanyi, Yao Yongkang, Guo Yongquan, Gan Caijin, Wang San, Chen Agen, Zhou Ayu, Pan Xikun, Tao Ada, Ying Jinyuan, Bai Yinxiao, Du Tongdou, and Han Xiaolin, and 25 other male and female gamblers were arrested on the spot, and mahjong tiles, poker cards, etc., along with gambling funds, silver coins, were seized and taken to the station. After being interrogated by Director Liu, the defendants claimed that the house was a vacant yard, Li Wangshi was the second landlord and there was no banker, and they were just relaxing during the Lunar New Year. They refused to confess the truth. Director Liu determined that there must be a banker because there were so many gamblers gathered in the den. In addition to ordering a secret investigation, he sentenced Li Wangshi and others as witnesses to be sent to the General Bureau for legal action.

Apprentice Actually Treats Boss as Son 187

Sends Intimidating Letter with Hundred Sheets of Tin Foil

Walks Right Into Trap, Admits to Extortion Unreservedly

Ren Chuntang, a 47-year-old Ningbo native, runs the Ren Chunji Laundry shop at the intersection of Haig Road and Hongqiao Road (Chinese territory), and his business is not bad, with some savings. An apprentice, Shi Fuguan, about 20 years old, also a Ningbo native, left and did not return on the 30th day of the intercalary fifth month of the lunar calendar last year. Another apprentice, Xu Genyuan, also left with Shi on the same day. Around December of the lunar calendar last year, Xu Genyuan suddenly came to Ren Chuntang to borrow 100 yuan. Ren replied that business was slow and he did not have such a large sum of money at the moment, but only agreed to lend him 50 yuan. Xu was dissatisfied and left angrily. The next day (January 20th of this year), Ren received an intimidating letter with threatening language, roughly stating that his son (referring to Ren as son) knew that several fathers (referring to the senders) were unhappy with him and he should be careful, and that his family's children (Ren only has one son, eight years old) should be careful. Ren ignored the letter after receiving it. Unexpectedly, he received two more letters, one on February 16th and one on February 19th. The third letter contained 100 sheets of tin foil, probably meaning to bring Ren bad luck. Ren carefully examined the handwriting and knew that it was written by Shi Fuguan. He was about to report it when Shi Fuguan walked right into the trap. He suddenly came to Ren's shop to make trouble and forcibly borrow silver coins. Ren immediately called the police and had Shi arrested at the Second Division of the Sixth District. Ren Chuntang presented the three threatening letters. Shi Fuguan confessed that he wrote them. He was instructed to prepare a document and send the accused along with the threatening letters to the local court for interrogation.

Boat Crew Member Crushed to Death by Mast 188

Boat owner Liu Guyuan, a native of Zhenhai, was transporting yellow sand from Huzhou to Shanghai. There were seven crew members on board. Yesterday morning, they were sailing at high speed when, while passing through the Luligang Puchun area west of Minhang, a strong north wind suddenly blew and the mast at the bow of the boat suddenly fell. One of the crew members, Xu Jin, (31 years old, a native of Funing) was tending to it nearby and could not avoid it. His head was crushed by the mast base, and his left temple was injured, causing a hole. He immediately fell and died, blood gushing out like a spring, lying in a pool of blood. The scene was extremely tragic. Boat owner Liu Guyuan ordered the boat to be sailed to Rihui Port and reported to the water patrol team, which sent police to temporarily detain another crew member, Zhong Wenlong. Liu Guyuan reported to the local court for an autopsy. It was stated that the deceased was recommended to work on the boat, with a monthly salary of nine yuan, and had only worked for about two months. Subsequently, Prosecutor Cao Changling questioned him and then led Examiner Xuan Zhiming to conduct an autopsy. It was found that the deceased Xu Jin was indeed crushed to death. The report stated that the boat owner Liu Guyuan should provide a coffin and burial, pending further investigation.

Arrest of Bandit Wang Sanzi 190

Last December, Chinese and Western detectives from the police station arrested bandits Yan Alan and Xu Asi. They also seized a box cannon, two .32 caliber pistols, and forty-four bullets from No. 20 Chongyi Lane, Malang Road in the French Concession. The two men were handed over to the First Special District Court. They confessed that their accomplice, Wang Sanzi from Jiangbei, was on the run and could not be apprehended. As a result, the two criminals were sentenced to imprisonment. At 7:20 AM the previous morning, Chinese Detective Wang Chengying from the Jiaxing Road police station apprehended Wang near Fuzhou Road and Zhejiang Road. He was taken to the police station where the chief ordered him to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was transferred to the Third Criminal Court. Lawyer Wang Yaotang from the Public Works Bureau recounted the events and requested that the defendant be temporarily detained for investigation into whether he was involved in other robbery cases in the Public Concession. When questioned, Wang Sanzi claimed to be 36 years old and residing on Songshan Road in the French Concession. He denied any knowledge of the firearms hidden at No. 20 Chongyi Lane, Malang Road, and pleaded for a fair judgment. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered him to be remanded in custody for further investigation.

Weather Report 202

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Shandong area is cloudy with strong northwesterly winds. The Yangtze River basin and this area are cloudy with rain or snow. The wind is from the north to the northeast. There are cyclones and rain in the East China Sea and Taiwan due to the passage of a low-pressure system moving eastward. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this area was 44.1 degrees, and the lowest was 38.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 44.2 degrees, and the lowest was 35.6 degrees.

Letter 204

To the Editor:

Having read the article "Wusong Party and Government Organs Mediate Rent Reduction" in your newspaper's local news section on the 22nd of this month, I find that it does not fully accord with the facts. In particular, the concluding statement "The problem of rent reduction has not been resolved" is untrue. I must request a correction to clarify the facts.

Our company has more than a hundred houses in Wusong City, which were destroyed in the January 28th incident last year. We were unable to rebuild them. Later, due to the encouragement of various parties who were concerned about the city's appearance, our company, in accordance with the municipal government's reconstruction plan, mortgaged all the land to Yiji Bank and勉力rebuilt thirty houses first. Based on the estimated cost, the rent was set at 20 yuan and 6 cents per house, which is the lowest price and barely covers the mortgage interest and expenses. On February 8th, when the four organs convened a meeting to mediate, we presented detailed accounts. After repeated review by the attendees, it was confirmed that no further reduction was possible. The original rent price was unanimously approved and recorded. As for other items, our company has had deep emotional ties with the tenants for many years, so we have all made concessions. Thus, the rent dispute has been resolved and there are no outstanding issues. Fearing that rumors will cause misunderstandings, I hereby briefly explain the situation and request that you provide a correction to clarify the truth.

Sincerely, Ren Changhe Real Estate Company, Shanghai. January 22nd.

How to Understand New International Terminology (1) 205

Reading Guidance:

According to a friend, the Reading Guidance is specifically set up for readers of the Shenbao Circulation Library, and its guidance scope is limited to the readers of the library. If this is true, I wonder if I, a poor boy stranded far away, can also be granted special consideration and guidance? First of all! I am very urgently seeking! I sincerely beseech the teacher to heal us illiterates and save us lonely and helpless youths with the spirit of teaching all without discrimination!

I am a Western-style clothing worker, currently working as a clerk in a Chinese-owned Western-style clothing store here in Japan. (Most of the Western-style clothing stores here are opened by Chinese.) When I was young, I read some books like "Hundred Family Surnames," "Thousand Character Classic," "Primer of Classical Allusions," and "Classic of Filial Piety" in a private school in my hometown for about three years. Later, because my family could not afford it, I had to be sent to a weaving factory in Hangzhou as an apprentice. The so-called apprentice actually learned not weaving technology, but rather换水烟袋for the accountant, sweeping the house, making tea, serving meals,倒便壼, catching臭虫, and other chores. After messing around like this for more than two years, I ended up returning to my hungry home due to a serious illness. Because of my poor health, my mother told me to learn a lighter craft. Tailoring only requires sitting and threading needles all day long, and it is 문축문하기. This was truly the most ideal and noble profession in my mother's eyes. And my destiny, my youth, was sewn into the needle holes of the clothes of those wealthy gentry and aristocratic sons. The ruler in my hand cannot measure my own bleak future. The so-called happiness, the so-called joy, has already been cut off by the scissors and彈去了 by the chalk line.

Teacher! Do you think what I wrote above is nonsense? No, this is enough to prove that people like me are everywhere, whether in remote rural areas or at the ends of the earth. Therefore, I hope that your work is not only targeted at shop assistants, workers, and unemployed youths in Shanghai.

Now, please allow me to state the main purpose of my writing this letter. In the past, I was also one of those沉沦in low-level taste, reading鸳鸯蝴蝶派 novels (as mentioned in Mr. He Chang's letter in your publication on the first of this month). However, in recent years, I have changed. I feel that these are harmful to my stomach, and I want to replace them with some nutritious things to solve my hunger. Now, what I want to ask the teacher to teach me is a part of this new food that I cannot digest.

I have recently become very fond of reading social science books, and I pay special attention to reading the newspapers. I can say that I read every word of the international news reported in the newspapers without missing a single one. I have gradually become clear about the changes in the international political situation, as well as the organizational systems of various countries and the主張of various political parties. But what I don't understand now is the news in the economic field, such as "currency war," "currency cooperation," "dollar devaluation," "American purchase of gold," "exchange rate stabilization guarantee," "gold embargo lift," "gold export," "gold policy," and other various terms that I cannot thoroughly understand. Teacher! Are there any popular books that can explain these questions that I can purchase? Or, how can I gain basic knowledge in this area and overcome my current difficulties in understanding? Can the books listed below help me solve the previous difficulties? I would like to ask the teacher to clearly teach me these things!

(1) "Research on the Problem of Gold Expensive Silver Cheap," (2) "Outline of Currency," (3) "World Currency Problem," (4) "Research on the Price of Silver," (5) "Currency ABC," (6) "Discussion on the Problem of Gold Expensive Silver Cheap," (7) "The Problem of Gold," (8) "World Economic Conference," (9) "Silver Problem" (see library catalog). Teacher, regarding the questions I raised earlier, I not only do not understand them, but I simply do not understand what relationship they have with the national economy and people's livelihood? Who is manipulating its changes? I really don't understand at all. Teacher, you won't laugh at me for being too naive, right?

In addition, I would like to systematically study economics. Please trouble the teacher to provide me with a list of books from simple to profound. I think that with the prescription the teacher has prescribed for me, I will definitely be able to build a strong physique. I offer my most sincere enthusiasm to the teacher.

(Letter from Chen Changxing, Tokyo)

Loving Spirit 206

— Jingjuan

Children: What is your school motto? Does it have the four words "Loving Spirit"? Are you loving towards your teachers? Do you have a loving spirit towards your classmates?

Foreigners say that we Chinese are like scattered sand without a loving spirit. Therefore, when foreigners invade our territory, we cannot unite to resist. Sometimes, we even fight among ourselves. This is because we lack a loving spirit.

Children: You must have a loving spirit towards your fathers, mothers, elder brothers, younger brothers, elder sisters, younger sisters, teachers, and classmates. You must also have a loving spirit towards every Chinese person in society. If we unite this great loving spirit, our country will have great strength as a whole. Would foreigners still dare to bully us? Would they still dare to ridicule us as a nation like scattered sand? Would we Chinese still be afraid of not being strong?

Children: Everyone must have a loving spirit!

Am I Not As Good As Them? 207

— Yin

Lingling is already seven years old. Her mother chose a school for her and sent her to enroll. But when she heard the news of going to school, she started to cry. Although her mother repeatedly tried to persuade her, Lingling was unwilling to go to school. She said, "Studying is not as fun as playing."

One morning, she secretly slipped out of the school gate and met a large squirrel on the road. She said to the squirrel, "You are so happy! Eating walnuts, drinking clear water, how free you are! I want to play with you and be permanent companions." The squirrel replied, "I don't have time. I have to find food for my children. I must work. Where would I have time to play?" Lingling had to find something else to play with. She met ants again. She said, "Brother Ant! Come and play with me for a while!" The ant shook its head and said, "Where would I have space? If I don't work, how can I live?" Lingling went to find bees. She said to the bees, "You are so happy! Singing songs all day long, flying around, looking at the scenery, let's be friends and play games?" The bee said, "I'm sorry, please find another friend! I have to work to get through the winter. There is no time for playing!"

Lingling thought: These animals all have to work, let me go find flowers to play with. They are idle all day and have nothing to do. So she walked up to a small red flower and said to it, "Little red flower! I think you are idle all day long and don't need to work. Play with me for a while." The little red flower said, "My work is very busy. Every day I have to open my petals, absorb sunlight and air. This requires my roots to find food in the soil, and then use my branches to distribute nutrients to all parts of my body. Where would I have any time to spare?"

After hearing the flower's words, Lingling immediately returned to her mother and said to her, "Dear Mother! Animals and plants in the world all have work to do. Am I not as good as them? I also want to do things!" Her mother patted Lingling's shoulder and said, "Little darling! Don't you also have work to do? Going to school to study is your immediate and important work!" After hearing her mother's words, Lingling became very diligent in going to school from then on.

Children! The season for school to start has arrived. Are there any of you who are playing truant? Let him read this fable, and perhaps he will become a hard-working child.

The Argument of the Year 208

— Li

It was very cold today. After dinner, Dad declared first that he wouldn't go out tonight. Then, Mom also declared that she wouldn't go out tonight. So we sat around the stove chatting.

There were four of us in total: Dad, Mom, me, and my little sister.

Dad kept looking at me and smiling. I thought to myself, he's going to tell a story again today.

Unexpectedly, Mom spoke first, interrupting this good thing. Mom said, "Last year was the Year of National Products, and this year is the Year of Women's National Products, and also the Year of the Child. Last year was your year, this year is my and Huier's year."

After Mom said that, she kept looking at Dad and smiling, and Dad was also smiling. I heard the words "Year of the Child" for the first time today. Although I didn't understand it, I was very happy because Mom said this year was mine and her year.

Dad said, "Your year, I'm afraid you won't get good results. Women are too vain, too concerned about looking good. It's Huier's year that will be more reliable. I believe many children will definitely welcome the arrival of this Year of the Child."

In this way, I was even happier.

Then, Mom said again, "How were your results last year in this year of yours?"

After hearing this, Dad didn't speak, as if he couldn't answer. Mom seemed very proud, as if she had won a victory.

After a long silence, I asked Mom, "What does 'Year of the Child' mean?"

Mom replied to me, "The meaning of the Year of the Child is that in this year, we will do more things for children, especially help children more, publish many children's books for children to read, improve children's lives more, and if we do well this year, if we have real results, then this year will be your happiest year!"

Two Animals That Save People in Winter 209

— Daqi

In the lost Northeast provinces of my country, the climate in winter is much colder than in the south. Often, people on the road cannot withstand the severe cold and collapse on the road, frozen stiff, and die from freezing. There is a kind of wild animal called a sable. If it encounters a frozen person on the road, it will gather many sables of its kind to cover the frozen person. Because the body temperature of the sable is very high, the frozen person often gets warmth and is saved. How loving and intelligent this little animal is! But there are people who catch sables who take advantage of this, pretending to be dead, lying on the road, waiting for many sables to save their lives. Then they get up, catch the sables one by one, and skin them to sell for money. Sable fur is very valuable, although they profit from it, but I think this behavior is deceptive and cruel. I really want to feel unfair for the sables, as the saying goes, "A good deed is not rewarded!"

There is a kind of dog in Europe that can save people who are lost in the mountains when it snows heavily, and help them safely descend the mountain, so they don't freeze to death on the mountain, and don't mistakenly walk and fall into a snow pit. This kind of dog is raised by people at the foot of the mountain. When it snows heavily, they tie a bottle of wine to the dog, and the dog runs to the mountain, delivering the wine to the lost person. The lost person drinks the wine and naturally feels warmer, able to resist the cold air, and can move. Dogs have the strongest memory. Even though snow covers the mountains and valleys, burying the paths, the dog can still distinguish the roads, leading the way in front, and the lost person follows behind, safely descending the mountain. Otherwise, in a dilemma, they would freeze to death.

Hua'er's Awakening 210

— Shicong

Ri'er: You guys, the piece of candy in Hua'er's hand is so big and so good, let's go and snatch it, what do you all think?

Ying'er: Great! Great! You go and snatch it, I'll help you.

Fa'er: Hurry up, don't let him run away.

Hua'er: Okay! You guys are snatching my candy, I'll go tell Lian'er.

Hua'er: Lian'er, Ri'er and the others are snatching my candy, can you please get it back for me?

Lian'er: Great! Great! But what will you give me as a reward?

Hua'er: If you get the candy back, I'll give you a piece of cake.

Lian'er: No, no, please give me the cake first.

Hua'er: Okay, okay, you take the cake first, but don't forget about the candy.

Lian'er didn't get the candy back, but ate the cake. Hua'er asked him to return the cake, but instead he hit him.

Hua'er lost the candy and the cake, and was very angry in his heart. From then on, he knew that only himself was the most reliable in the world.

The Child Without Hands 211

— Yan Chonglou

There is a child next door to my house. Because he was very naughty, he was playing next to a boiling pot of water one time. He was careless and his upper body fell into the pot. The boiling water scalded him half to death. Later, although he was cured by a doctor, his two hands eventually became disabled!

Every day when he gets up, he needs someone else to dress him; when he washes his face, he needs someone else to wash him; when he eats, he needs someone else to feed him;... He sees other children being able to write square characters, draw pictures, do handicrafts,... He can't do these things himself; he envies others on the one hand and resents himself on the other! He often thinks: "I now know the happiness of having hands." But he will forever be a disabled person!

Children! Do you think this child without hands is pitiful? But if you don't use your hands, how are you any different from this disabled child!

Jokes 212

— Zhang Xing Su

(1) Borrowed in a Dream

Mary asked her brother George to return the copper coin she lent him.

George said, "I didn't borrow it!"

Mary said, "Are you trying to deny the debt? Didn't you borrow it from me in a dream?"

(2) Thermal Expansion and Contraction

The younger brother asked the older brother, "Why is winter vacation shorter than summer vacation?"

The older brother said: "Summer vacation days are longer, winter vacation days are shorter, this is the principle of thermal expansion and contraction."

(3) They Always Hit Where It Hurts

The younger brother's left hand was broken, and the mother put a Band-Aid on it for him.

The younger brother said, "Mom, put it on my right hand."

The mother asked in surprise, "Why don't you put it on the broken left hand?"

The younger brother replied triumphantly, "You don't know, they always hit where it hurts."

(4) Older Brother is So Stupid

The older brother said to the mother, "Last night I had a dream and dreamed that the table was full of biscuits."

The younger brother said, "Older brother is so stupid, why didn't you bring a few to me to eat?"

(5) One Hundred Points

John said to his mother, "I got one hundred points on the test today!" Mother asked, "What subject was it?"

John said, "Chinese fifty points, math fifty points."

Animal Smiles 214

— Bing Yu

Humans generally show smiles when they are happy. There is an old saying that goes, "When the heart gets what it likes, the mouth always wants to laugh." Animals are the same. When animals are happy, angry, sad, or happy, although they don't have expressions like smiling and crying like higher-level humans, even if they do have expressions, our human eyes can't tell the difference. But what we often see is just the appearance of muscle tension and relaxation. For example, when they are happy, animals will definitely show their teeth, a joyful appearance. The following expressions can be shown: (1) All teeth can be seen, (2) The lips are contracted, (3) The tip of the nose is wrinkled, (4) Unconsciously emitting a slight sound, (5) Eyes are moist? (6) Light and unrestrained appearance. Such as lions, tigers, leopards and other feline beasts, are like this. If it is a bird, it will call out a slight happy sound. Generally, the calls of birds, probably high-pitched calls are singing, and low-pitched calls indicate what they want. If we are often close to birds and beasts, we can tell the difference. For example, when feeding, the birds and beasts are naturally very happy, and show a lively smile. When competing with their kind, they show a fierce angry expression. When they are afraid of being harmed by different kinds, they show a sad expression with elongated muscles and trembling.

Snow Reflection Song 215

— Hua

Sun Kang is poor, Sun Kang is poor, but he studies hard, never stopping day and night. The weather is cold, the snow falls, the world is like inlaid silver. The rich, bake by the stove sweating profusely. The poor, wrapped in rags cold and ice. You are also afraid of the cold, so cold that you don't say a word; everyone is afraid of the cold, so cold that they don't go out; everyone is afraid of the cold, so cold that they have no spirit. Sun Kang! He also wants to study hard, but only because he doesn't have a lamp.

Suddenly I saw a bright light outside the window, why not catch snow as an oil lamp. Sun Kang does it, makes it happen, piles up layers on the table, white snow piles shining brightly, reflecting the snow light to study hard. Ah! Reflecting the snow light to study hard.

Alas! Why don't children with lamps study hard?

The Progress of Communication Devices | From Waving to Wireless Telegraphy 216

— He Gongchao

The sound of human speech can only be heard within a few steps; when two people are far apart, they cannot hear each other. However, people cannot avoid separation, nor can they avoid communicating messages to each other. Therefore, our ancestors came up with ways to greet each other from afar very early on. Humans in the Stone Age waved to greet each other when they were separated by a river or a valley (Figure 1). Or burn a pile of fire (Figure 2) to let the people on the opposite side know that there are people here too. Later, beacon fires were invented (Figure 3). When enemies invaded, they raised bright beacon fires to warn the people in their territory to prepare quickly. We have probably all read the story of "King You of Zhou Playing with the Dukes with Beacon Fires" in history. From this story, we can know that beacon fires were the only means of communication at that time. In the eighteenth century, the French created a Venetian blind-style communication device (Figure 4). This thing was erected in high places, one every four or five miles. There were six leaves that could be opened and closed freely. Due to various different opening and closing methods, sixty-three different symbols could be expressed. This communication device was later improved by the British, becoming something like a signal machine on modern railways (Figure 5). They erected this kind of signal machine in important locations everywhere to convey military news. However, it was completely ineffective at night and in foggy weather. At the same time, in the army, soldiers used a kind of disc (Figure 6) as a signal to communicate messages. In the nineteenth century, a heliograph (Figure 7) appeared, which used the flash of light reflected from a mirror to transmit messages. In 1837, the American Morse invented the wired telegraph. His earliest telegraph machine used needles to indicate numbers (Figure 8), and was gradually improved to become what it is today (Figure 9). In 1877, the Englishman Bell invented the telephone (Figure 10). Finally, Marconi invented the wireless telegraph (Figure 11), which is the most convenient tool for modern communication.

Ke Lai's Head Work 228

As soon as the rain started, Jinan had the ambition to take the lead. Luo Haiguang and Fu Hexuan, two generals, peeked at the opportunity twice without success. Kao Sitan sat in the central hub and commanded calmly. Pike was temporarily transferred because of the fatigue of Mai Shanaier. The defensive robbery in the rear guard and the transportation were extremely skilled. After dozens of rounds back and forth, Xiao Huate obtained the Remidi triangle pass, and even trapped the heavy defense, breaking into the vicinity of the low line. He kicked it into the center, and Ke Mai said that the head was spiritual, and it flew diagonally into the net with a bang.

General Fu Raised Troops for Revenge 229

After Jinan lost a goal first, it aroused indignation. Chen Zhenxiang crossed the defense zone to help the forwards and advanced with drums. Xuan Xiong gained power and smashed the door, but unexpectedly it was blocked by Fulusou, and Fu's shot finally hit the mark.

Baoxiutuo's Quick Shot Made a Contribution 230

After the autumn colors were evenly divided, the audience was all happily pleased, as if Jianan had the possibility of winning. So they shouted in unison and cheered for them. However, the thickness of the strength is the touchstone. Fortunately, Xu Heng and Gu Shangxiang were inside, and they were still able to turn danger into safety many times. However, the wise men had a thousand worries, and they were bound to make a mistake. French Merchant Team Wins Three-on-One 231

Seven minutes later, the Jinan team, with all five forwards advancing, was about to create another tie. Unexpectedly, a silver whistle blew, signaling the end of the half. This Year's Graduates Allowed to Continue Their Studies

Shandong Education Department Revises Regulations for Subsidizing Students Studying Outside the Province 242

Yesterday's Letter Notified Shandong Students at Universities in This City

The Shandong Provincial Education Department sent a letter to universities in this city yesterday, stating that the regulations for subsidizing students studying outside the province have now been revised and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and filing. However, the number of subsidies for this year has already been approved. The regulations will be implemented according to Article 2, Section 2 of the regulations next year. A copy of the regulations is enclosed for your university to review and inform Shandong students accordingly. Attached: Revised Regulations of Shandong Province for Subsidizing Students Studying Outside the Province. Article 1: In order to cultivate specialized talents most needed in the local area, this province has established Shandong student scholarship quotas in the departments of various universities and specialized schools outside the province. The number of quotas shall be determined by the Education Department when preparing the budget each year. Article 2: Students eligible for the scholarship are those who are studying in undergraduate departments of national, provincial, or registered private universities and specialized schools outside the province and whose grades are above 70 points. The allocation of quotas for the aforementioned schools and departments (those belonging to science, engineering, agriculture, medicine, etc. shall not be less than three-quarters of the total quota) shall be formulated by the Education Department at the beginning of each year and submitted to the provincial government for approval. Article 3: The scholarship is set at 100 yuan per person per year. Article 4: Student grades shall be based on the academic year grades of the previous academic year, but first-year students may use their admission grades as the standard. Article 5: Students who suspend their studies and then resume them, as certified by the school, may still use the grades of the academic year before the suspension as the standard. Article 6: Students who transfer to another school may use the grades of the previous academic year from the original school as the standard. Article 7: If the number of students with academic year grades or admission grades above 70 points exceeds the scholarship quota, the Education Department shall grant the scholarship to those with better grades. If the grades are equal, the scholarship shall be granted to those in higher grades. Article 8: The scholarship shall be issued in two installments each year by the Education Department to the school where the student is located, which will then transfer it to the student and send the receipt to the Education Department. Article 9: If a student receiving a scholarship graduates and leaves the school, and the scholarship for the final academic year has not yet been claimed, the student may, with proof from the school, directly apply to the Education Department for a supplementary payment, which is limited to two months after the Education Department's notification is issued. After the deadline, the payment will be stopped. Article 10: Students receiving scholarships have the obligation to be entrusted by the various departments of the provincial government to investigate special events. Article 11: If a student has one of the following circumstances, as verified by the Education Department or certified by the school where the student is located, the scholarship will be stopped immediately: (1) those who have counter-revolutionary remarks and actions; (2) those who suspend or withdraw from school; (3) those who are absent from class for more than one month without reason. Article 11: Students who have obtained subsidies before July 19 of the Republic of China shall be handled in accordance with the Provisional Measures for Reorganizing Overseas Study Affairs in Shandong Province and shall not be subject to the provisions of these Regulations. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in these Regulations, the Education Department shall revise them at any time and submit them to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for the record. Article 14: These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation.

Jiangsu Education Director Zhou Fohai Addresses Elementary School Teachers Throughout the Province 244

Implement Local Education to Achieve the Goal of National Education

Zhou Fohai, Director of the Education Department of Jiangsu Province, addressed elementary school teachers throughout the province with the title "Implement Local Education to Achieve the Goal of National Education." The original text is as follows:

Dear teachers, in this period of foreign aggression and at this critical juncture for the survival of the nation, only education is our method of salvation, and only elementary education is our fundamental method of salvation. Therefore, our elementary education must undergo major reforms, and our elementary school teachers should have a deep awareness. The purpose of education in our country has always been to "enrich people's lives, support the survival of society, develop the national economy, and continue the life of the nation." However, every nation has its own special environment, so every nation should have its own special education in order to promote its inherent national spirit and continue its national life. Therefore, nationalistic education is the basis of education, especially the basis of elementary education. Because elementary school children are the life cells of the nation, only healthy cells can lead to a healthy life. Implementing nationalistic elementary education means cultivating healthy national life cells and continuing the nation's eternal life. Therefore, from the perspective of the purpose of education in our country, nationalistic elementary education is the policy that we urgently need to implement. Moreover, the crisis of our nation cannot be resolved in the short term, and the struggle of the nation should be prepared for in the long term. In the long-term preparation (

), nationalistic elementary education should be the fundamental preparation, and the final victory or defeat of our nation depends on the success or failure of nationalistic elementary education. Looking at the Franco-Prussian War, where Prussia was able to defeat France, and the Russo-Japanese War, where Japan was able to defeat Russia, the world attributes the success to the elementary education of Prussia and Japan, which is well known to everyone. Even the Xinhai Revolution was due to the fact that the idea of anti-Manchuism had long been instilled in the minds of elementary school children. Therefore, the Wuchang Uprising was launched, and the Qing Ming rule was overthrown. There are countless examples of this. Therefore, from the perspective of the current national environment in our country, nationalistic elementary education is an urgent task. Looking back at the past elementary education in our country, it was not uncommon to take patriotism and national salvation as its purpose, and it was not uncommon to take the cultivation of patriotic ideas as its goal. But what has been the result of more than 30 years? Once national disaster strikes, how many people in the entire nation can automatically sacrifice themselves to save the country? How many of those who are able to truly awaken? On the other hand, traitors who kill their compatriots for foreign enemies and foreign slaves who act as lackeys for foreigners are everywhere. This is certainly a painful thing for us, and at the same time, it can reveal the mistakes of past education. Because past education, although it had a certain direction, neglected the importance of implementation. It only instilled empty national ideas without cultivating deep local love. Beliefs were not established and the foundation was not solid. Once tempted by foreign objects, internal shaking began, so traitors and foreign slaves were more numerous than patriotic people. As a result, past patriotic education failed. Learning from the mistakes of the past, we should seek practical corrections. Therefore, the implementation of nationalistic education must take local education as a prerequisite in order to have a solid foundation. Because the cultivation of national thought should be based on the concept of localism. Without a love of home, national thought is like an illusion. Without local education, national education loses its roots. A long journey must begin with a short step, and true love must come from personal experience. Therefore, implementing local education is a prerequisite for implementing national education.

The task of local education is to inspire children's knowledge of their hometowns and cultivate children's love of their hometowns. However, in order to make them cherish their hometowns, they must first make them understand their hometowns. Therefore, inspiring children's knowledge of their hometowns is also the first step in local education. There are approximately three methods of inspiration. First, children should be made aware of the history, monuments, great men, and past sages of their hometown, so that they can develop a heartfelt admiration for the past of their hometown. Second, children should be made familiar with the current geography, products, customs, habits, economy, transportation, and life of their hometown, so that they can gain a true understanding of the present of their hometown. Third, children should be made aware of the advantages and disadvantages of their hometown, so that they can have reform ideals for the future of their hometown. Once the understanding of the three is clear, the emotion of the hometown will naturally arise.

As for the relationship between hometown and nation, it is originally the relationship between the whole and the part, which is also a mutually dependent relationship. Once there is an understanding of the hometown, and then with considerable inspiration, it is easy to gain an understanding of the nation. Once there is a love of hometown, and then with practical guidance, it is easy to develop a love of nation. This connection of organic relationships is also the function of local education. Human love is originally from small to large and from near to far, so those who can understand their hometown must be able to understand the nation, and those who can love their hometown must be able to love the nation. Looking at the past dynasties of our country, when bandits and chaos disturbed the country, if there were a few people who sacrificed themselves to defend their hometowns, the overall situation would be maintained. Another example is when Japanese pirates invaded Jiangnan, and if there were occasional loyal and righteous people who sacrificed themselves to defend their hometowns, the nation would be spared from being invaded. It can be seen that those who can directly protect their hometowns can directly protect the nation, and those who directly love their hometowns indirectly love the nation. This is enough to prove that national thought must be based on love of hometown, and national education should be based on local education.

However, the implementation of local education is by no means a revival of feudal thought. Because the local education that we advocate takes nationalism as its goal, and the worldism of the Three Principles of the People is based on nationalism. Therefore, the nature of local education, in the near term, is the foundation of the nation, and in the long term, it can be said to be the starting point of worldism. The importance and urgency of local education are as described above. Therefore, in the essentials for the improvement of elementary education that this department promulgated last year, it was stipulated that local teaching materials should be implemented, and now education bureaus in various counties have been ordered to organize local teaching material compilation committees to promote its realization. Therefore, at this time of striving to implement local education, there are several urgent (

) hopes for you:

(1) Strive to implement local education with nationalism as the goal and truly understand the true meaning of national education.

(2) Conscientiously assist the local teaching material compilation committee of this county in conducting local investigations and contributing opinions.

(3) Conscientiously study the content of local teaching materials to obtain correct teaching.

(4) Conscientiously study the teaching methods for implementing local teaching materials.

(5) Strive to further study general academic theory as an aid to the implementation of local education.

The above are my hopes for you, and they are also your duties. It must be known that without implementing national education, elementary education is tantamount to waste, and without implementing local education, there is no way to realize nationalistic education. Therefore, the success or failure of local education is not only related to the rise and fall of elementary education, but also to the survival of the entire nation. The stakes are high, not just for the sake of formalities. The responsibilities that you bear are especially important. I hope that you will not underestimate yourself, do not be perfunctory, and work together to accomplish this major mission.

Regulations for Overseas Chinese Primary and Secondary Schools Revised by the Ministry of Education (Continued) 245

Eighth Child Students,

Article 38: Children of overseas Chinese who have reached the age of six shall attend overseas Chinese schools. Graduates of primary schools may enter secondary schools. In areas where there are no secondary schools, they may enter nearby overseas Chinese secondary schools or return to China to continue their studies. The methods for returning to China to continue their studies shall be determined separately. Article 39: Students who have completed their studies in overseas Chinese primary and secondary schools shall, in addition to taking graduation examinations by the schools, submit a list of the students who have passed the graduation examinations and their grades in each subject to the competent consulate within ten days for the joint examination. The regulations for the organization of the joint examination committee and the detailed rules for handling shall be determined separately. In special circumstances or in areas where there is no consulate or where the consulate is too far away, the functions of the joint examination may be exercised by local or nearby overseas Chinese education groups that have been registered by the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. If a joint examination of overseas Chinese education groups has not been established, or if there is only one overseas Chinese school in the area, the joint examination may be waived. However, the graduation examination papers of secondary schools that are exempt from the joint examination must be sent to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for review. Those who pass the joint examination or review shall be issued graduation certificates by the schools, which shall be presented to the competent consulate or the joint examination committee for verification. Secondary school graduation certificates shall also be presented to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for verification. Students who have completed the term of study in junior primary school and whose grades are passing shall be issued graduation certificates by the schools and may be exempted from the joint examination. Article 40: The methods for students to pay fees and for poor students to be exempted from fees shall be determined by the competent consulate in consultation with the local overseas Chinese education group and shall be submitted to the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for record and implementation. Chapter Nine, Academic Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates,

Article 41: The academic year, semester, and holiday dates of overseas Chinese primary and secondary schools shall be handled in accordance with the "Regulations for Revising School Academic Year, Semester, and Holiday Dates" stipulated by the Ministry of Education in areas where the climate is the same as that of the country. In areas where the climate is different from that of the country, the academic year, semester, and holiday dates may be handled in accordance with the academic year, semester, and holiday dates of foreign schools in the area. Article 42: Special commemorative days in the location of overseas Chinese primary and secondary schools that are stipulated by the local government and must be closed may be closed as usual. Article 43: Overseas Chinese primary and secondary schools shall not take holidays arbitrarily except for Sunday holidays, commemorative holidays, special commemorative days in the location, and school commemorative day holidays. Various gatherings shall be held on Sundays. On revolutionary commemorative days, except in special circumstances, they shall be handled in accordance with the concise table of revolutionary commemorative days promulgated by the National Government (promulgated by the National Government in July 19 of the Republic of China).

Chinese Vocational Education Society Expert Meeting 246

More than Thirty Attendees Including Gu Yinting and Tao Zhihxing

Organizing the National Revival Education Design Committee

Proposals on Production Education, etc., to be Published in a Declaration

The Chinese Vocational Education Society held its eighth expert meeting yesterday starting at 9:00 AM at Huxi Weichang, Caohejing. More than thirty attendees including Gu Yinting discussed over ten important proposals. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Attendees: Gu Yinting, Tao Zhihxing, Huang Renzhi, Liao Maoru, Yu Qingye, Chen Jicheng, Ou Yuanhuai, Li Gongpu, Tang Xiongbo, Jiang Wenyu, Pan Xulun, Wang Zhixin, Chen Liren, Chen Qingshi, He Qingru, Xiong Zirong, Wang Kuilun, Wang Zhaoki, Cheng Shaojiong, Shao Shuangqiu, Huang Qisheng, Jia Foru, Zhao Aiwu, Shi Yangyong, Feng Ying, Huang Nian, Pan Yangyao, Li Chucai, Zheng Wenhan, Wen Chonglu, Xie Xiangzhi, Yang Chongang, Zhang Xuecheng, Wu Cuilun, Wuyin Fo, Yang Ziqiang, and others, totaling over thirty people.

Reported Matters: The meeting commenced at 9:00 AM with Jiang Wenyu reporting on the purpose of the meeting. Gu Yinting, Liao Maoru, and Yu Qingrong were elected as the chairing committee, with Wu Cuilun as the recorder. Regarding reported matters, He Qingru reported on recent research and editorial work, Jia Foru reported on the current situation of the Chinese Vocational School, Jiang Wenyu reported on the current situation of vocational supplementary education and the general situation of various schools jointly operated by the Society, Zhao Aiwu reported on the current situation of the Second Supplementary School and the Nanjing Road Commercial Supplementary School, Pan Yangyao reported on the current situation of the vocational guidance center, Jiang Wenyu reported on the current situation of rural affairs, Lu Shuang reported on the current situation of the Xu Gongqiao Rural Improvement Association, and Huang Qisheng reported on his past experience participating in rural education work, investigating the feelings of the Northwest countryside, and his views on rural education.

Discussion of Proposals: Proposals were discussed at 1:00 PM. (1) Should the General Meeting of Members of this session predetermine central issues? Resolved: The results of today's discussion will be compiled by the Society's office into central proposals for the General Meeting of Members. (2) Should the Society specifically raise and discuss several matters within the scope of vocational education that are considered most urgent at present? If the discussion reaches a conclusion, the Society will earnestly promote experimentation and request the government to advocate them. Resolved: The opinions expressed by everyone will be separately submitted to the Ministry of Education and research institutions for cooperative handling. (3) Huang Renzhi proposed the establishment of a National Revival Education Design Committee. Resolved: Passed. Gu Yinting, Yu Qingtang, Liao Maoru, Tao Zhihxing, Tai Shuangqiu, Huang Renzhi, Pan Yangyao, Jiang Wenyu, Zhao Aiwu, Chen Liren, Li Gongpu, and Huang Qisheng were elected as committee members. (4) How should the Society train vocational guidance talents? and (5) A proposal to use the Shanghai Guidance Center to handle guidance affairs for various schools. Resolved: Request the Ministry of Education to establish a vocational guidance training institute, instructing provinces and cities to send personnel to study. (6) Should the Society organize an inspection group to visit the vocational education situation in various regions? Resolved: The Ministry of Education will send personnel to investigate education in various provinces, and the Society can request to join. (7) Practical measures to relieve unemployed youth. Resolved: Amended and passed. (8) How to conduct unemployment statistics. Resolved: Submit to the government for handling. (9) How to regulate youth work-study programs. Resolved: Amended and passed. (10) How to guide employed youth to work with peace of mind. Resolved: The opinions expressed by everyone will be handled by the vocational guidance center. (11) If occupational opportunities can be predicted. Resolved: Gather various opinions and publish a declaration on the Society's views on vocational education and production education, etc. The declaration will be drafted by the Vocational Education Society. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM after the discussions.

What is said is the result of daily research and practical experience, and students benefit greatly. In addition, the senior high school normal second grade, the simplified normal third grade, the senior high school commercial first grade, the junior and senior high school general departments, and the primary school departments at all levels have vacancies and can still be inserted into classes.
