Women's Garden

Where Are Women Going? 252

— Yuan

I remember that in the six or seven years after the May Fourth Movement, discussing women's issues was a very fashionable thing; but now, it is said that partly because the women's issues that have been discussed for several years have not reached a more concrete conclusion, and partly because the focus of modern social problems seems to have shifted to another place, so everyone has to put the problem aside for the time being; and in this period of shelving, women are still feeling depressed and wandering; the braver ones, like flies hitting glass windows, are stubbornly confronting the old society, and the outcome is of course hard to say; and the weaker ones can only endure the pain and let the waves of the old society engulf them.

On the eve of the Great War, the waves of individualism swept the women of the world, and at that time what they demanded was "freedom," but they did not think that freedom required an economic element as its foundation; therefore, this slogan did not even need reality to teach a lesson, and it was already known to be an empty cry, and the free marriage and free divorce issues that have been troubling for several years, and the comedies of other sexual relationships, were nothing more than interludes on the eve of the world's economic depression.

If women want to obtain the same social status as men, they can only obtain the economic status that is the foundation of everything in the same way as men. The term "professional woman" may be fashionable in modern times, but professional women who sincerely want to obtain economic status still feel the pain of hitting walls everywhere under the current social system. The conflict between career and housework has obviously become the maze of all progressive women; according to the current facts, to be a professional woman, one must give up the right to form a family; otherwise, one can only be a dim housewife for life.

However, progressive women are absolutely unwilling to let housework determine their lives; therefore: to obtain economic independence; to have a career, one has to give up the right to have a family, and has to live a lonely and bitter life, and even a kind of mental abnormality occurs: all families are treated with malice.

Modern women are being burned in the sparks of this conflict.

In fact, the existence of this conflict is not objective, nor is there no way to avoid it.

Regarding this issue, the British sexual psychologist Havelock Ellis said it very clearly in an article titled "The Future of the Family," and one section is worth quoting:

"::: Women should appropriately allocate their time and energy to both family and society, so that both aspects can have a development that was previously unattainable. In the Soviet Union, women's social equality has been fully realized according to XX's original intention || XX said: "Every housekeeper should know a little about politics." Many women in the Soviet Union have a high social status on the one hand, and are housewives on the other; the state stipulates that they (referring to all women || author's note) are given two months of leave before and after production, and there are nurseries and educational gardens to share their maternal responsibilities, and their salaries are still paid during the breastfeeding period. From this, it can be seen that the incompatibility of motherhood and social career in other countries is not necessarily impossible, it is just that stubborn habits and blind prejudices are at work."

Here, Havelock Ellis clearly points out, and cites iron facts to prove: women's careers and families are not objectively conflicting, and the main factor that creates this conflict is "stubborn habits and blind prejudices."

But these "stubborn habits and blind prejudices" cannot be underestimated, they represent the entire feudal and unreasonable social system.

For themselves, for mankind (women are the mothers of mankind, this cannot be denied, right?), the only place for women to go in the future is to unite with all those who are dissatisfied with the current social system, and all those who are being squeezed by the current social system, to strive for a more reasonable social system. 2, 1, 33.

Women's Vocational Skills 253

— Guizhong

Naturally, no one can deny that if the entire society is in a state of chaos, then women's issues will never be properly resolved alone. However, we cannot stop talking about women's liberation due to the inferiority of social phenomena. On the one hand, we must naturally connect women's movements with social issues. On the other hand, we should try to solve some individual women's issues anytime and anywhere. These two things are mutually supportive.

So, what is the most noteworthy issue in our current women's movement in China? The so-called "women's suffrage" and "inheritance rights" are very high-level demands, and most women still have to sigh.

I think: If we need to further liberate the majority of women, then "women's occupations" is an important issue at present:

The phenomenon of women depending on others because they lack considerable vocational skills, or selling their bodies, is becoming more and more serious every day || If this continues, will women's social status not fall further into the dark abyss? How much attention should every person who cares about women's issues pay to remedy this heartbreaking phenomenon!

Although the "unemployment" panic is a widespread social phenomenon at present, it is even more serious for women. This is because women themselves lack vocational skills. For example, many female employees who work in institutions are called "vases" because they are not capable enough. And the so-called "vases" sell their looks and smiles to their superiors because they are afraid of being incompetent, which is also a very common thing. In order to remedy this unemployment panic that is even more serious for women, we can only start from enriching women's vocational skills!

I think that in the future, every educated woman should plan her own family's economic strength, and be able to receive what kind of education within this scope, and prepare for a skill of her own. As long as she can be competent in a job, it does not necessarily mean that she must go to university. We have seen many college students without skills eventually fall.

As for the vocational skills of female workers and peasants, enthusiastic women's activists need to run more reading classes or schools for workers and peasants to improve their cultural level, and at the same time teach them various crafts, bookkeeping and other skills, which can also be remedied in case of emergency!

Progress in the Indian Women's Community 254

— Wenyin

India is a country of religious fervor. Traditionally, various religions have given women a rather respected position, both in the family and in society. According to their legends, the original text of a certain scripture in Indian religions was written down by women. Even today, Indians continue to worship Saraswati as the goddess of learning. However, it was only in the last twenty years that Indian women became aware of themselves and began to take an interest in their social status.

At the beginning of this century, India produced many famous noble ladies. They began to form organized group movements around fifteen years ago. The earliest women's group was the Indian Women's Association, founded in 1917, led by Dr. Annie Besant. Now the association has a total of seventy-two branches, and its members are all over India. The end of this organized women's movement enabled women in the Indian Union to obtain civil rights and suffrage.

The All-India Women's Conference, founded in 1926, is one of the most powerful groups in the Indian women's community recently. It has more than 180 electoral districts in various states. The conference includes representatives of various classes, races, and religions. Domestic science research associations, women's vocational schools, and female teacher training institutes in various places are all affiliated undertakings organized by this group. In addition, there is also the Women's National Conference, whose headquarters are located in Bombay (Baviye). There is also the University Women's League, which is organized by women's student associations who have graduated from various universities, and has a deep interest in understanding social life and international situations. In various places, there are also many local women's associations. The women's groups mentioned above have made considerable efforts and achievements in social undertakings such as education, health care, and relief. Some groups also devote themselves to eliminating linguistic segregation in various places, and promoting or rewarding their country's unique arts and various crafts.

Currently, there is a female member in the state council of Travancore State in India, who also serves as the state's health director. A female member also served as the acting chairman of MacDonald's Legislative Council. They strongly advocate for the promotion of women's education, the establishment and promotion of medical relief organizations for women and children, the eradication of various bad habits of women, and the prohibition of early marriage, and hope for their implementation. There are also many knowledgeable women who are engaged in the administrative organs and educational institutions of various cities.

Many educated and talented women bravely participate in the national movement that is sweeping India, and fight for the liberation of their motherland and the liberation of the Indian nation. For example, Mrs. Salojini Naidu was imprisoned twice, and Mrs. Consins, the former secretary of the Indian Women's Association, was also imprisoned for opposing the emergency disciplinary regulations and has not yet been released. Kamala Devi, the first secretary of the same association, was also imprisoned twice for participating in political activities. Over the past ten years, Indian women have been solving their own problems from self-consciousness, and now they have gone a step further, rising up to fight imperialism politically in order to liberate their motherland and liberate the Indian nation. This progress is indeed a good example and is worthy of our learning from.

A Woman's Life 256

— Xuanwen

2. First Menstruation

The first menstruation of a woman usually occurs between the ages of thirteen and eighteen; due to the relationship between climate and race, there are differences in the time of occurrence.

The symptoms at the beginning of the first menstruation vary due to physical constitution. Some come suddenly without being aware of it, while others feel heaviness in the lower abdomen and waist for several months, and the breasts are particularly sensitive before menstruation comes.

A careless mother does not notice the physiological changes in her daughter, letting her be surprised and sad, and unknowingly developing a dim impression of sexual knowledge.

When a girl has her first menstruation, the mother should not make her do excessive labor. On this day, it is the birth festival of her new life, and a celebration ceremony can be held for her to show a happy memory.

Regarding teaching how to deal with menstruation, the mother should explain in detail. If there is no correct method in practice, she can give her books on how to deal with menstruation, which is also a good method.

The proper procedure for dealing with menstruation: First, use more cotton wool, so that the menstruation will not soak through or stain clothes, and will not cause nervous fatigue. The method of using cotton wool is to cut it into appropriate sizes, fold it into several layers, and replace it or add new cotton wool as soon as it is stained with menstruation. The ideal time to exchange each time is two hours. At this time, it is necessary to pay attention to cleanliness, and neither unclean grass paper nor long-term non-replacement should be used.

There are also various types of menstrual belts, and there are advantages and disadvantages in terms of application. For example, rubber ones do not soak through, but they are not very washable, and cotton ones are prone to leakage, but the latter is more economical than the former.

Avoid strenuous exercise and overwork during menstruation.

It is not advisable to take a bath during menstruation, especially not to wash with dirty water, lest bacteria enter the vagina and cause accidental danger.

During menstruation, especially for girls with first menstruation, it is very easy to be moved by everything, and the spirit is also particularly easy to be excited, and the expression of joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness is also particularly obvious, so at that time, the mother must pay attention to keeping her spirit calm.

Correspondence 257

Mr. Reporter

"Women's Garden" has opened up a place for us women to freely express our opinions, which is very meaningful, because although it is now the so-called Republic of China, women also have a very small number of roles in politics and society, but in terms of quantity and quality, they are in a very unimportant position, and it cannot be said that women's issues have been resolved in any way. So, what way should we take to solve the current women's issues in China? I think the first is the education issue, the second is the economic issue, and the third is the political issue. Because if the education issue is fully resolved, we will have the skills to live, and if we have the skills to live, the economic issue can naturally be resolved; if the economic issue is resolved, we can live independently, and then participate in political movements, and naturally there is nothing to fear. Following this path, we will probably not lose sight of the grand goals, or lose sight of empty talk. What do you think, sir? It is fortunate to have your teachings, not just for one person. Zhu Ruhong

February 21

I have carefully read your letter. You can propose a way to solve women's issues when the world is drunk and dreaming, which can be called an extraordinary statement. Although women's issues are complicated, the main points are no more than the three points you mentioned. However, there is room for discussion on the order of priority of the three points you mentioned. From the understanding of common sense, naturally, the education issue must be resolved first. National scholars and doctors have said a lot about it in the past two or three decades. However, it is important to know that the foundation of education lies in economics, and its reliance on progress and maintenance without being corrupt, or development and glorification, lies in politics and economics. Therefore, if political and economic issues are not fundamentally and generally resolved, and it is said that the education issue for women can be fully resolved, who will believe it if it is not an idiot?" Then, your opinion that "the education issue" is the first step in solving women's issues is not a discussion of the root cause. As for the economic and political issues, in basic terms, economics comes first, but if you want to fundamentally solve economic issues, it is absolutely impossible without making a clear move in politics. This is increasingly believed by recent events. Therefore, we now use political transformation as a sharp tool to solve economic problems, and economic transformation as the purpose of completing political transformation. Women's issues cannot be separated from the entire social issues, and general social issues cannot be resolved, just as women's issues cannot be resolved, and general society cannot be said to be resolved. Generally speaking, it has to be like this. A hasty answer, not all, what is your opinion? What about the opinions of the general public? (Reporter)

Ellen Key and Alexandra Kollontai (Continued) 258

— Purple

Fei Pei: What was Ellen Key's view on love?

Purple Prose: She advocated for love based on the unity of spirit and flesh, and the whole personality. In other words, it is the mutual love and harmony of two people, male and female, who stand on the same parallel line in terms of body, knowledge, and morality. The two are one, and this kind of union can live forever in the furnace of love.

Ying Ying: I think this is completely ideal, no wonder she had to remain single her whole life.

Purple Prose: Ellen Key advocated that marriage does not need formality. She said that between two sexes, if there is pure and sincere love, there is naturally noble morality, and there is no need to borrow laws to protect it. At the same time, she also advocated unconditional divorce. She said that love is not permanent. When there is absolutely no love between the two sexes, everyone should break up to avoid superficial harmony and mutual pain.

Ying Ying: This can only be regarded as an ideal, and we hope that this ideal can be realized. But the facts do not make us so optimistic, especially in the current Chinese society, in a male-centered society, although marriage does not need to have any grand ceremonies, it is best to go through legal procedures to avoid irresponsible people, who change their minds in the morning and evening, and take love as a game.

Fei Pei: What about Ellen Key's theory of motherhood?

Purple Prose: She advocated that men and women should have different duties and fulfill their respective responsibilities. The core of a woman's domain is to be a mother, so if a woman cannot fulfill her duties as a mother, even if she can fulfill her duties in society, she cannot be said to be a "complete person."

Purple Prose: Next, we have to talk about Alexandra Kollontai.

Fei Pei: Is Alexandra Kollontai still alive?

Purple Prose: Yes, she is already sixty-two years old this year, but according to people who have seen her, if people did not know her age, they would think she was a young lady. Her father, General "Domontovich," was a large landowner in the old Russian era. He was very stubborn, so Madame Kollontai's life as a child was very restricted. The thought of liberalism was very popular in Russia at that time, and her father was afraid that she would be infected with this thought, so he did not allow her to go to school, but only allowed her to study hard at home. But people are often very strange. Under such rigid education, her resistance would be more obvious than ordinary people. At the age of eighteen, she participated in various social activities.

Ying Ying: It is said that she knows several languages. Is that right?

Purple Prose: Yes, her footprints have traveled all over Europe and the Americas. At first, she graduated from the University of Zurich in Germany, studying organization theory, and later she studied anthropology and sociology. She has her own unique views on labor issues, women's issues, etc. At the same time, she also has twelve points of accomplishment in literature. During the Russian Revolution in 1917, she was also one of the key figures, and was therefore arrested and imprisoned. After the success of the revolution, she was elected as a member of the Central Committee of the Bolsheviks. In 1923, she was appointed as the ambassador to Norway and the commercial representative, opening a new record in the history of world diplomacy for female diplomats.

Fei Pei: What are her views on women's liberation?

Purple Prose: She divides the past and future social phenomena into three eras: (1) In primitive people, men hunted, herded, and went on expeditions, without a fixed residence. Women are in charge of raising children, and engage in farming, preparing food, and making clothes for raising children. At that time, everything was centered on women, which is the so-called "era of matriarchy." (2) After that, life became stable, men dominated production, and controlled all economic power, and women became subordinate to men. This is the so-called "patriarchal era." Women are just childbearing machines, playthings of men, and can be bought and sold with money. (3)

Due to the development of capitalism, craftsmen, small businessmen, and farmers have lost their original land and are engaged in mechanical work, but low wages are not enough to support their wives and slaves, so wives and daughters have to engage in production themselves. Because women's wages are lower, it is generally easier to hire them. Women who have been excluded from the production sector have returned to the same field as men. Since women have the same economic field as men, they naturally advocate equal rights. This is the real "era of equality between men and women." Kollontai once said, "The so-called legal wives who are supported by men, do not engage in production, and entrust their children to servants for raising, and spend their days in consumption and enjoyment, can only be regarded as prostitutes."

The Securities and Bond Markets are Enveloped by Rumors 264

Disarmament and the Customs of '19 Fell by More Than One Yuan

Full-Day Trading Resumes on the 27th

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange still only traded for one month in March. The market announced that the futures trading for April will be allowed to start trading on the market from the 27th, and the four-session trading for the whole day will be resumed. Yesterday's trading was still not lonely, but the market price has not yet recovered. There are rumors in the market that the United States' increase in the price of silver will affect my country's tariffs, which is inevitably a nervous reaction and too early to say. Some believe that the situation is still not appropriate, the Sun rebellion is getting worse, and the bandit rebellion is getting more and more serious, which is still a superficial view. There are also rumors of organizing short-selling companies, which is not in line with English. Only by organizing a company can there be common interests, which is not possible for the general public. People are selfish, or they wait for the price to sell, or they take the opportunity to sell, fearing to fall behind, how can they unite? Therefore, such rumors are self-defeating. In fact, the initial rise in the market price was slightly sold by the initial slight strength, and then it caused the speculators to short sell. It was expected that the market price would fall by about one yuan. At this time, when the silver root is loose and the floating capital is abundant, the financial community will not sell goods for money unless there is a special reason. Therefore, the future will not suddenly lead to a sharp fall. Yesterday morning, when the market opened, No. 16 and No. 38 were quite sold, and long positions also came out. Retail short selling in the market also gradually surged, and the market price suddenly fell by one or two cents to half a yuan. The second session caused retail long positions to seek to get rid of, disarmament suddenly fell by seven cents, and the rest also continued to fall by three or four cents. However, the salt tax gradually rose due to the gradual rise of the eating households, and the short gold of the whole six also turned good by one cent. Once the wind returned, the overall situation was set. As a result, only the Customs of '19 fell by one yuan and one cent, and the disarmament fell by one yuan and five cents the most. The rest mostly fell by two or three cents to six or seven cents. The total number of transactions was 7.207 million yuan, including 2,000 yuan in spot goods and 7.205 million yuan in futures. Improvement in the Underlying Position of U.S. Cotton 269

A telegram from New York on the 23rd reports on the cotton market for the week, stating: At the beginning of the week, the cotton market's initial approval of the Pinhai Plan failed to stimulate buying. Selling was due to large-scale profit-taking by bulls and a lack of urgent needs from fellow traders. However, it later reversed course due to extremely thin shipments from the South. Currently, people are extremely uncertain, as the House Agriculture Committee is delaying a final decision on the Pinhai Plan, and the final terms are difficult to predict. However, President Roosevelt has already endorsed the plan, and there is widespread hope that it will result in the passage of some form of mandatory management. It is believed that there is some "dime cotton" in the South that will be sold if the futures price reaches 12 cents or more, but its supply will be absorbed. Fellow traders are buying on price dips, so the underlying position has improved. At the same time, the arrangement of new cotton is faster than usual.

Cheaper Pricing for Imported Wheat; Downward Trend in Forward Flour Market Spurs Widespread Selling by Mills 270

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, market conditions for various months were generally stable. The quoted price for imported wheat was around 1.23 to 1.8 cents lower in Chicago and 0.8 cents lower in Canada. Therefore, after the opening, the current month saw a slight softening, and forward months also felt weak. Subsequently, due to mills selling off inventory, the market turned to wait-and-see. The market was somewhat empty, and there was some covering, so while trading remained active, market sentiment was slightly stable. When the market opened in the afternoon, the current month's market hovered throughout the day with little fluctuation. Forward months, however, fell sharply across the board, as news spread that Argentine wheat was priced even more loosely, reportedly at only $4.10 (five cents cheaper than the previous day). Shin Da Hua Feng and Xinda jointly chartered a ship, leading to a surge in market selling. Fufeng's sales were particularly robust, causing forward months to fall another cent across the board. As a result, the current month saw no change, March fell by half a cent, April and May fell by 1.5 cents, June fell by 2 cents, and July fell by 2.5 cents.

Nearby Wheat Stable, Forward Months Weak 271

Yesterday's futures wheat market saw nearby months stable and forward months weak in both the morning and afternoon sessions. Due to imported wheat quotes from Chicago and Canada only rebounding by about 0.8 to 1.23 cents, trading remained light after the opening. However, as the current month was the last day, requiring delivery after this point, although overall volume was low, bulls were mills with intentions to take delivery. Hua Feng was expected to take delivery of over 20 truckloads, supporting prices. June and July did not open in the morning. In the afternoon, the sentiment softened due to new imported wheat deliveries, and prices opened lower. As a result, the current month was better by two cents, April better by two cents, June down by a small two cents, and July down by a small three cents. The spot market was still good at the end, but the market was only so-so. Dong wheat opened at $3.42, and Bengbu wheat at $3.32, then at $3.30, totaling 1,000 bags, which Fuxin purchased.

Rice Prices Remain Relatively Calm 272

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, supplies from various sources were relatively abundant, with a total of twenty to thirty groups (over three thousand people) arriving. Sales in various markets were stagnant and unresponsive. Urban and rural stores made some purchases due to the recent rain, but the volume was limited. If sellers raised their prices slightly, buyers immediately hesitated, making it difficult for the market to improve. Common, Suzhou, and South Port type japonica rice remained flat, and Do-Yang pointed rice also saw little fluctuation. As for Qingjiao, Songsi, Xilian, and other late rice varieties, merchant brokers, such as those from the North and South Ocean groups, continued to trade 1,400 to 1,500 bags, but also due to the uneasy sentiment and overall weakness of the market, there were no significant gains or losses, and prices remained unchanged, with the exception of the Yin Yuan variety, which felt slightly tighter due to a shortage of goods.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, thirty-one or thirty-two boats arrived from various routes along the river. Sales of all goods in the market were sluggish and stagnant. The market showed flat prices for high-quality white japonica, Yang-pointed, and early rice, and slightly cheaper prices for medium and lower grades, close to a few cents lower. Thin rice was also slightly softer. The prices for White Yuan, Yin Yuan, Do-pointed, and Bu-pointed remained stable.

Hunan Coarse Red Rice Falls Another 2 Cents 273

Yesterday, guest Xian rice continued to arrive at the docks, and there were even more en route. This was because at the end of the lunar year, inquiries came from Quanzhou, Fuzhou, Xinghua, Xiamen, and other groups in Fujian Province. The market was initially expected to improve, and many sought supplies from the producing areas to ship to Shanghai. Currently, demand from Fujian has waned, and there is no active demand from the local or Zhejiang groups, leading to nervousness among guest traders seeking to sell. The market immediately saw another decline. The stock of Hunan red coarse rice was sufficient, and owners were even more eager to sell. Prices had already fallen by about half a yuan in recent days, and yesterday saw another small 2-cent drop. A thousand bags were shipped to Fuzhou at a price of $5.48 to $5.45. Fuzhou also took 540 bags of Shashi coarse rice at a price of $5.40, also down slightly. Quanzhou took 400 bags of Hunan machine-pressed oil rice at a price of $7.32. The local street took 154 bags of Nanjing machine-pressed Xian rice at a price of $6.40. The local street, along with the Ningbo group and others, traded over a hundred bags of Jiangxi machine-pressed Yuan rice at prices ranging from $7.40 to $7.35. Overall, coarse red rice fell by a small 2 cents, while other varieties fell by a small cent or so.

Vigorous Sales of Soybean Cakes in South China 274

The destination for soybean cakes is mainly South China and the interior. With convenient shipping routes to various locations in South China, buyers directly procure goods from the production areas. Therefore, the amount of cake shipped from this city to South China last year decreased by one-third. Recently, the price of cake in this city has been cheaper compared to other ports, attracting inquiries from Shantou, Xiamen, Fuzhou, and others. Yesterday, the total number of cake transactions in the overall market was around 60,000 to 70,000 pieces, to be delivered in about two weeks. The reason is that current cake factories need to deliver the futures cakes that are due. If current cakes are needed, merchants will resell their goods.

Northern and Southern Goods: Orchid Seeds, High-Quality Goods in Short Supply 275

Orchid seeds, especially high-quality ones, are scarce and the supply is not continuous. The market is stable. Sales from various parties have been active in recent days, so quoted prices have been tightened. Several dozen boxes were offered, with prices ranging from $32-33 to $30, but those with black color still lacked buyers. It is reported that if there are goods that are completely yellow without sand or stones, the current market price can be raised to $34-35. Current sellers have already telegraphed the producing areas to urge loading.

Silk and Tea: Pingshui Green Tea, American Merchants Report Price Drops 276

The Pingshui green tea from Shaoxing and Ningbo in Zhejiang province, last year the sales volume to America was no less than 80,000 boxes. As of the end of last month, American tea merchants still had 20,000 to 30,000 boxes in hand. Previously, merchants made small profits from sales of pearl tea, needle tea, and eyebrow tea. Recently, due to the U.S. government's proposed increase in silver prices, sentiment has become unstable. Merchants are eagerly seeking to sell their holdings. The selling price of pearl tea has plummeted by $5 per hundred pounds, and other teas have also fallen by $3-4. This kind of unstable situation has had a significant impact on Chinese tea.

Metals: A Large Batch of Japanese Tacks Arrives in China 277

The small tack market has loosened due to news of a large batch of Eastern goods arriving in China. The market standard has been loosened. Currently, Western goods are sold for $26 per barrel for 3-penny tacks, $17.5 for 4-penny, $15.5 for 5-penny, and $13.5 for 6-penny. For factory goods, 4-penny is quoted at $16.5, 5-penny at $14.5, and 6-penny at $12.5. Actual transactions are reportedly cheaper by about 3-4 cents. Transactions are still good on Changjiang Road, but there are no confirmed orders on North Road besides inquiries. There is still a lot of business in this street, but it is fragmented. It is reported that about 500-600 barrels of Eastern goods will arrive at the beginning of next month, causing great panic in the market. It is found that the cost of Eastern goods is mostly $12-13 (stripped), which makes the Shanghai market even weaker.

Amateur Weekly

Amateur Musings

What a "Lifetime Occupation"! 299

— Gongpu

One afternoon last month, a calm and composed young friend brought a letter of introduction from Mr. Pan to see me. Mr. Pan used to be an English professor at Northeastern University. After reading the letter, I learned that this young man's surname was Lu. He was a graduate of Northeastern University. Before and after the September 18th Incident, he taught at a middle school in Harbin. Later, unwilling to live the life of a subjugated people, he resolutely joined the Volunteer Army to engage in anti-Japanese work. After the defeat at Yimianpo, he came to Shanghai hoping to find some work. Who knew that after living there for several months, the money he had brought was used up, and there was no work to be found. He fully experienced the pain of unemployment. After the reporter talked with him, he asked him to write down his feelings about being unemployed for several months as a reference for introduction. The next day, he turned in his paper, titled "My Lifetime Occupation." The words were filled with courage and unyielding spirit, and the pure and frank self-description was a special feature of this article. A friend said that there were quite a few radical tones in the article. Shouldn't they be slightly deleted? Alas! I only felt that it was a very pure confession of a young man who lost his job due to resisting Japan, worthy of song and tears, lovable and respectable! If people are not understanding and make malicious guesses, then the reporter will have to stop writing from now on. The following is Mr. Lu's original text, attached behind without any changes, as a substitute for casual talk. "The economic panic, like a storm, swept the globe, followed by the wild waves of unemployment, surging like the autumn tide, countless people, fell into the icy abyss of hunger and cold. Today, it is like the end of the world.

The unemployment of ordinary people is either due to being laid off or being excluded. But I, who originally had a "high salary and generous benefits," gave it up "willingly."

It seems that I "willingly gave it up," but every person in my situation, if he has blood, he will not admit this sentence, and will resolutely protest. The fact is this: Originally, I taught at a middle school in Harbin, with a monthly salary of more than two hundred yuan, which cannot be said to be not extremely abundant. However, after the September 18th Incident, Northeastern education was completely enslaved. Although I could still receive the same "high salary and generous benefits," I was unwilling to be a prisoner of the enemy, so I "willingly gave up" my original occupation and joined the ranks of resisting the enemy. Although I endured the wind and snow, and the difficulties of life were beyond my wildest dreams, I did not feel bitter, but rather at peace. However, in the Battle of Yimianpo, with ammunition exhausted and reinforcements cut off, after several days of support, I finally had to retreat in tears. From then on, my good hometown was no longer a place for me to settle down. I had no choice but to escape to Shanghai, which was said to be the most激昻 place for national movements, after several risks. When I arrived in Shanghai, I could still see our government's slogan of "long-term resistance" and the high-sounding argument of "internal pacification must come before external resistance" in the newspapers. However, I never saw or heard of how to assist those who were resisting the enemy, or how to provide relief to those who were injured or killed because of resisting the enemy. Shanghai, the center of the national movement, was shrouded and confused by "wine, women, song, and horses." At the same time, I also became unemployed in "isolated helplessness." This is the process of my willingly giving up "high salary and generous benefits," and also the cause of my falling into the icy abyss of hunger and cold.

I have tried in many ways to find an occupation to make a living, and to prepare myself to realize my long-cherished aspirations. However, even if I am willing to "cheaply" sell my flesh and blood for others to exploit, no one wants me. I do not believe that a person who has received higher education is of no use to society. If higher education is useless, then why are countless universities still producing countless college students? I am willing to serve society, so why does society "abandon" me? Could it be that so-called "talent" is also "overproduced" like commodities? Then why is it that the Soviet Union's productivity exceeds that of the current capitalist countries by several times, and yet there is not a single unemployed person? These are all the feelings that have accumulated in me since I became unemployed and failed to find a job. Now, although I have lost a "high salary and generous benefits" and cannot find a job that can even make a living, I have not given up. On the contrary, I have seized a lifetime occupation, which is to serve the truth, dedicate myself to justice, strive for national liberation, and fight for the future of mankind. Facts tell us that only by overthrowing the current unreasonable society can there be a way out and light. And this kind of unreasonable society will inevitably collapse due to the "tendency of accumulation of the capitalist system." Today is the end of the capitalist world, and now we are just short of driving it into the grave. This is my occupation, my lifetime occupation."

Life

Doing Full Moon 300

— Bei'an

Every night, after eating my fill of boredom, dragging my tired body, stepping on the dirty streets, I squeezed into my nest. My wife always greeted me with a smile and comforted me in every way. Therefore, everything from the day suddenly disappeared. In the lonely and miserable path of life, my wife is truly my only comforter. I am very grateful to her. However, in recent days, her attitude has been a little strange. Her eyebrows are tightly locked, as if she has something important on her mind. When I chat with her, she is always strange. I finally couldn't bear it anymore and asked her:

"Hui! Why has your attitude changed? Do you have something important on your mind?" She jumped up, pointed her finger at my forehead, and said hatefully:

"You've lived to be so old, and you're still like a little child, not thinking at all. Your sister is getting married, don't you know? Although the gifts have been sent, according to the custom in the countryside, we still have to do a full moon." "What is doing a full moon?" I asked deliberately.

"Dumbass! You don't even understand this. After getting married, after a full month, you send things over, that's called doing a full moon." She replied sadly.

"What kind of things should we send?"

"Two fresh hams, six hundred round cakes, four bundles, and forty eggs."

"How much money will it cost to buy all these things?"

"At least ten dollars."

"Ten dollars!" I couldn't help but be stunned. My salary is only fourteen dollars a month. I am already worried about not having enough for food, clothing, and housing on weekdays. Where would I have extra money to do this kind of empty thing? I don't want to do things that are all about saving face and suffering. So I said to her:

"My sister was given away to someone else when she was young. Now that she is getting married, we can just use our own means to send some gifts. We can save on the other customs."

"You have a bit of a pig temper. I'm telling you something serious, and you're always like this. Don't you care about face? Aren't you afraid of people criticizing you? I'm a little embarrassed. People always think it's my idea." She said angrily.

"I don't have this kind of extra money. I don't care. You can do it if you have money." I also said angrily.

A small house that was usually harmonious was filled with worry in an instant. Outside the window, it was dark, and the north wind was howling. It seemed to be sneering at our poverty.

"I knew you would say that, so I didn't tell you. You don't have to worry about it. Give me this month's food expenses. I'll go back to my parents' house for a month. Use this month's food expenses to buy things for the full moon." 静

Page 20

After a long silence, she said this to me.

I was a little unwilling to agree with her proposal, but I was too embarrassed to object again, lest there be a rift between the couple, so I had to reluctantly agree. Now, my wife has been back home for six days. Every night, when I return home, the house is so quiet that you could catch ghosts. Desolation and loneliness surround my heart.

Anecdotes of Celebrities

Anecdotes of Mussolini 301

— Translated by Zhu

Once, Mussolini went to a theater to watch a movie. When he arrived, the movie had already started, so he had to enter the theater unnoticed in the dark and sit in the back rows. One of the films being shown depicted a solemn event that took place in Rome during the Fascist era. Mussolini himself had participated in this event. When the Mussolini in the film appeared on the screen, the general audience, in accordance with Italian custom, stood up solemnly, but the real Mussolini remained seated. So, people in the theater began to whisper to each other, violating the custom. A national guardsman was about to step forward to interfere with the troublemaker who did not stand up, when the bold theater owner, fearing that things would escalate, ran to the gentleman who remained seated, and in an angry tone loudly told him to stand up immediately so that everyone in the theater could see him. But then he leaned over and whispered to Mussolini, "You know, everyone here doesn't want to stand up just like you, but you'd better stand up."

Science and Technology Talk

Sun Wukong's "Stratosphere" 302

— Guangdou

A long time ago, we heard that three Soviet aviators had ascended into the stratosphere, setting a new world record. On January 31st, Reuters suddenly reported that the personnel who had ascended into the stratosphere had unfortunately met with disaster. The telegram read: "The Soviet authorities officially announced that the balloon chamber of the stratosphere balloon that ascended yesterday (January 30th) at 5 pm had been discovered in a village called Baodi, 200 kilometers from Moscow. The three aviators were all killed inside. One face was blurred and difficult to recognize. It is said that when the balloon was descending, it was suddenly attacked by a storm. The balloon's bladder broke away from the chamber and floated away. The chamber fell suddenly. When it landed, there were two loud explosions. The instruments installed in the chamber were all blown up." According to a radio station near Kotigomir, the last telegram received from the stratosphere balloon read: "Stratosphere balloon telegraph, the balloon has entered the blizzard zone, the surface of the balloon is all ice, we are in a desperate situation, two colleagues are dying." It can be seen that this accident probably occurred in the blizzard zone. Naturally, this is a loss to the aviation community.

But what is the stratosphere? Is ascending into the stratosphere an easy task? What kind of spectacle does our earth present when viewed from high altitude? Can people live up there? What are they doing in such high skies? These questions were asked by my little sister after reading the news above. Now, avoiding astronomical terms, let's "read the sky"!

It is said that the realm of the stratosphere is 16 kilometers above the ground. Except for Mr. Sun Wukong in Chinese "fiction," who once somersaulted and actually flipped to that place, few people in the world have ever been there. On August 18, 1932, a Mr. Picard once observed the stratosphere in a large balloon, but the records he brought back were still very limited. However, the exploration made by the Soviet Osavajim Stratosphere Balloon has achieved precise observations, especially in terms of optical success, which will have a huge impact on navigation. According to the Soviet Central Meteorological Bureau's observation results of the balloon, the changes in the color layer of the sky are as follows: 8.5 kilometers is sea blue, the next kilometer is dark blue, 13 kilometers is dark purple, 19 kilometers is dark purple sea blue, 21 kilometers is black purple gray, 22 kilometers is black gray. Other reports have not been released, so let's "hold on" for now.

Enough idle talk, let's get back to the topic.

It is said that the stratosphere is a kind of high altitude mentioned above. The color of the sky varies layer by layer according to its altitude. The color of light is probably ten times darker than seen on the ground. However, the sun's rays are stronger than on the ground. The air is so thin that it is about one-tenth of what it is on the ground. If you were magically sent to such a high place, all the fluids in your body would evaporate like opening a soda bottle. The reason is simple: The inside of the soda bottle is originally sealed with high-pressure gas. When you open the bottle cap, the hissing sound is due to the sudden decrease in pressure. The human body is the same. Soda that has lost its fizz will become ordinary water, bland and tasteless. The blood in the human body is subjected to this kind of evaporation, and the various organs will stop working.

But it is indeed very beautiful up there, like a slightly black monochromatic painting. When viewed through a magnifying telescope, through a thick layer of fog, the mountains, rivers, forests, and huge buildings on the ground become ridiculous and toy-like models. In good weather, you can see the shape of the earth, but you cannot see the stars.

After listening to the above, you will know that "going to heaven" is not an easy task. Currently, there are three ways to "go to heaven": airplanes, balloons, and rockets. Rockets are still far from practical use. Airplanes also cannot ascend to a height of 16 kilometers (about 10 miles). So the most suitable tool is the balloon. It has no vibration from the engine, no magnetic interference, and can ascend high.

Have you seen a hydrogen balloon? At least you have played with balloons that children play with. However, what is used here is a gas-draining device used in submarines, creating a small laboratory-like hanging basket. The hanging basket is connected to the balloon body, either with a net or with straps. The air in the hanging basket must be the same as on land so that the person ascending can live. Because there must be a constant supply of fresh air, gas-draining is used. It can emit half a gallon of pure gas per minute and send 20 gallons of air to the potassium, so that the potassium absorbs the carbon dioxide produced by breathing. The hanging basket is tightly sealed. The world inside is completely isolated from the outside world, but the person sitting inside is not Robinson. He is constantly using the radio to communicate with people outside.

As soon as hydrogen is injected into the balloon, the head of this magic ball rises and leaps upward into the sky. There is no cloud, rain, wind, or electricity in the good world of about 50 to 76 degrees Fahrenheit below zero. But the Soviet aviators encountered danger this time in the hail zone, probably more than 100 degrees below zero.

Although "going to heaven" is so difficult, this difficulty is gradually being overcome by science.

As for "what are they doing in such high skies?" Naturally, they are not playing like we "climb high on the Double Ninth Festival," nor are they purely gambling or curious, but are researching cosmic rays, because this is still a problem that humans do not understand very well. What is the purpose of studying cosmic rays? In short: to conquer the sky. If the stratosphere air route is once opened, the world will undergo huge changes! At that time, Europe and the Americas will shrink into two neighboring families. It will only take six to eight hours, and a lover in New York can visit a girl in Paris. Despite the gloomy weather on the earth's surface like in London, we fly in the clear blue-purple sky, without the troubles of the lower world. This is what we could only obtain in myths before, and now it is inevitably being realized day by day.

Of course, conquering the sky at present also has the meaning of controlling the sky and gaining air supremacy. It is also a matter that cannot be ignored in military terms.

Special Articles

The Crisis of Chinese Silk and Its Impact 303

— Ji Ling

The silk industry is one of our major national industries. Its annual export value accounts for more than 20% of total exports, worth tens of millions of taels of silver. If it were not subjected to external blows and internal destruction, and could develop smoothly, its future would be limitless. Unfortunately, since the global economic crisis of 1929, due to competition from countries such as Japan, France, and Italy, the resistance to artificial silk, and our own subjective destruction (such as exorbitant taxes and levies, floods, and wars), China's silk industry has declined day by day, even to the point of complete bankruptcy. This situation is very evident in the steadily decreasing numbers of Chinese silk exports since 1928:

Year Chinese Silk Exports (Unit: Dan)

1928 180,186

1929 189,980

1930 151,429

1931 131,186

1932 78,219

At the same time, the market price of Chinese silk has also been decreasing day by day. Since 1928, the decline in its market price has shown the following trend:

1928 1929 1930 1931 1932

December December December December December

High-Grade White Silk Warp (Unit: Dan) 1,847 1,726 1,518 1,451 1,036

(Unit: National Currency One Yuan)

By last year, the export of Chinese raw silk had decreased even more significantly, and its market price had fallen to around 500 yuan per dan.

As a result, silk factories have suspended operations, and the entire silk industry is in a state of bankruptcy.

China's silk industry is mainly centered in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. There were originally more than 180 silk reeling factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, with over 48,000 silk reeling machines. However, last year, fewer than 20 silk factories were operating in Shanghai, and only six were operating in Wuxi. Recently, almost all of them have shut down.

In addition, the silk industries in Guangdong, Sichuan, Shandong, and other places have suffered from various "natural and man-made disasters" and have fallen into a state of irreversible decline.

The decline and even bankruptcy of the silk industry have resulted in an increase in the number of unemployed workers, leading to a social crisis. In Jiangsu and Zhejiang alone, there are recently more than 600,000 people unemployed due to the closure of silk factories.

Secondly, the silk weaving industry has been affected by the decline of the silk industry. Due to the dumping of Japanese silk and its silk products, the sales of Chinese silk fabrics have almost completely disappeared. Even the markets in the Nanyang Islands have recently been seized. As a result, silk weaving factories have also had to suspend operations one after another. In Shanghai, only five are currently able to barely operate!

Furthermore, mulberry planting and silkworm rearing are the main side occupations of our country's farmers. In recent years, due to the decline of the silk industry, countless tragedies have occurred in rural areas due to the failure of silkworm rearing. Farmers in Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, and other provinces have even converted mulberry fields to opium cultivation because silkworm rearing is unprofitable. Even in Jiangsu, mulberry fields are gradually decreasing. According to a survey, Jiangsu still had 251,000 mu of mulberry fields in 1930, but by 1932, it had decreased to 84,000 mu. In this way, not only is the rural economy further bankrupt, but this bankruptcy can also reversely affect our silk industry and all other industries and businesses.

From this, it can be seen that the crisis of decline and bankruptcy of China's silk industry is not only related to the future of silk and all national industries, but also to the fate of our entire national economy and our entire society.

Anecdotes

The Barbecue Master and the Porter 304

— Translated by Zi Ming

In Paris, in front of a barbecue master's shop, a porter was eating his bread while smelling the aroma emitted from the barbecued meats. In this way, he felt that the bread had a fragrance and tasted very good.

The barbecue master did not stop this behavior. However, when the entire loaf of bread had been swallowed, he grabbed the porter's collar and demanded payment for the fragrance.

The porter replied that he had not caused any damage to the barbecue master's barbecued meats, nor had he taken anything from him. He did not owe him anything. The fragrance dissipated into the air, and it obviously disappeared. No one had ever heard of anyone in Paris being asked to pay for the fragrance of barbecued goods.

The barbecue master objected to the porter's words, saying that he had also never heard that he should use the fragrance of his barbecued goods to feed these people. He declared that if the porter did not pay him immediately, he would confiscate the porter's staff, carrying pole, and other belongings. Hearing these words, the porter seized his staff and put himself in a defensive state.

Both sides argued fiercely. The curious people of Paris gathered around, and John the Madman, known for his quick wit throughout the city, happened to be there.

The barbecue master saw John the Madman and asked the porter:

"Are you willing to let John resolve our dispute and be our judge?"

"Yes, I am willing," the porter said.

Both parties told the old John the whole story of their dispute. After listening, John asked the porter to take out a small silver coin of some kind from his pouch.

The porter put a small silver coin worth five francs into John's hand.

The madman took the silver coin, and with a serious expression, placed it on his left shoulder, as if to check its weight. Then, he moved it close to the pupil of his right eye, as if to see if the pattern on it was genuine. Later, he lightly tossed it on the counter, making it sound, many times, as if he were checking whether it was made of good silver.

While the madman was doing all these actions, the onlookers were silent. The barbecue master was preparing to put the small silver coin into his pocket, while the porter's face showed a sad expression.

Finally, the old John, with the authority of a court president, held the small silver coin in his hand, tightened the hat on his head, coughed two or three times, and spoke loudly:

"This court now makes this judgment: The porter, although he ate bread surrounded by the aroma of barbecued goods, has now paid the barbecue master with the sound of his silver coin. In addition, this court orders everyone to return to their own homes and waives the court fees."

The verdict of the Parisian madman seemed so just, so admired by the generally knowledgeable, that they did not even believe that any Parisian or Roman court could have had a better judgment.

From this, it can be known that a little bit of cleverness and quick wit is often equal in value to rich learning or knowledge.

Humorous Short Pieces 305

— Yamamoto

Drunkard A asked Drunkard B:

"Have you had breakfast today?"

"No, I haven't even had a drop."

○　○　○　○

Judge to defendant: "I ask you, why did you beat up five policemen?"

Defendant – a strong man – replied: "This is because I had good intentions. If I had only beaten one policeman, then he would have been beaten to death by me."

○　○　○　○

Hostess: "Minna, how can you tell that this hen is old?"

Maid: "From her teeth, Madam!"

Hostess: "Fool! Hens don't have teeth!"

Maid: "But I do!"

○　○　○　○

Professor: "In my opinion, this question is too difficult."

Examinee: "No, Professor; it's not that the question is difficult, but the answer is difficult."

○　○　　○　○

A gentleman said to his friend: "If your child cries loudly at night, then your wife can sing him to sleep."

His friend replied: "We have already tried this method, but the neighbors asked us to let the child cry instead."

○　○　○　○

On the streetcar, a wild child sat next to a very elegant lady. His nose was very unclean. Because of this, the lady asked him:

"Don't you have a handkerchief?"

"Yes, I do, but I don't lend it to strangers."

○　○　○　○

A: "Today I went to the doctor for a consultation because I often have problems with a weak memory."

B: "What did the doctor do?"

A: "He asked me to pay the medical fee in advance."

○　○　○　○

The telephone rang in the school, and the professor went to answer it. Professor: "This is Professor Miller."

Caller: "I have something to report. Carlo cannot come to school today because he is sick."

Professor: "I am very sorry to hear this. I wish him a speedy recovery! - May I ask who is speaking?"

Caller: "This is my father."

Literary Works

Shadow of Self-Destruction 306

— Li

On a picture album, I glimpsed the Elephant Trunk Hill of my hometown for no reason. I do not know whether it was the artistic eye of the photographer, or deliberately to ridicule me, this image happened to cut off a building, a pagoda, and a cluster of picturesque maple forests? I am too familiar with this scenery, which was the holy place where I paid homage morning and evening a few years ago. The owner of this place is Mr. Qingshui. The red building in the corner facing the river is the place where Mr. Qingshui's beloved daughter, Feiying, reads and paints, and Feiying seven years ago was the person who was never separated from me day and night. After a long separation, it has been seven years now. It is said that Mr. Qingshui passed away a long time ago, and what about Feiying? It is said that she has become the mother of three children. Originally, the passage of time has made that relationship fade day by day, until this year, even a faint silhouette is no longer in my mind. I didn't expect this mischievous picture to be sent to my eyes today, which can't help but make me relive an old dream and ignite the infatuation that I have suppressed for seven years.

It was also on a dim night with continuous wind and snow, that I returned from the north. As soon as I stepped on the soil of my hometown, I met Feiying in a lecture by chance. Although a friend specially introduced her at the time, saying that she was a high-achieving student in a provincial high school, and could paint a clear and vigorous ink bamboo, how could this ordinary social encounter make a forgetful memory capture her beautiful figure?

The second time we met was in the park. This was especially due to coincidence. Probably because one of her girlfriends was my in-law. This time we had a pleasant conversation for two hours. She naturally recognized me and knew a little about my background. The topics of conversation mainly revolved around the situation of schools in Beiping and the level of academics. She seemed to pay special attention to her own English, and she repeatedly asked twice what level of English was required to enter university. I can't recall any other words after that.

Because her father and my uncle were old classmates, he found out about my return and soon came to visit. As soon as he met me, he pleaded with my uncle to ask me to take some time to teach his daughter English for a month or two. Because of my uncle's order, I couldn't refuse.

I remember that on the day we started the class, because I wanted to know her level first in order to decide on the teaching materials, I started with an exam. Unexpectedly, her level had exceeded the "Great Prophecy" standard, which surprised me. But she didn't believe it. In the end, we still decided on a prose book as a reader, and also assigned several modern novels and an English weekly as reading material. Because she already had the ability to self-study, in the process of teaching, there were only literary conversations, and no need for sentence-by-sentence explanations, which made me feel an indescribable joy.

We gradually had a common interest and a blending of temperaments. We moved towards love day by day.

I still remember that when we were facing each other, we were silent for half an hour, and we couldn't think of a suitable word to cover up our mutual understanding. As a result, both sides blushed and deliberately avoided it. We were both cautious people, and neither side dared to reveal a hint. The bud of love was suppressed, but the flame in the heart burned to the extreme because of this pressure. Our only way to vent was to express it in writing. I remember that my diary that year had an unprecedented increase in length.

Good things are often difficult. In the spring of the second year, I had a long journey, and her high school life had not yet ended at this time. In fact, she could not leave the province to go to college. We could only endure a temporary separation.

I was so cowardly that I didn't dare to accept her love, which made her suspicious, thinking that I had another beauty in my heart, and that I didn't want to abuse love. This hurt her heart; at the same time, she had even more passionate respect for me. She almost destroyed herself for me.

I taught in a certain place for two years. Because of the unrest in my hometown, I had no intention of returning home, but just wandered, wandered, wandered. But at first we still had a constant mailbox, and after half a year it decreased. After another year, I learned that she was engaged to a certain university student. Last year, I heard that she was the mother of three children.

Now, looking back, it is like a dream. We were so in tune with each other, why did I have to avoid and escape? Since I wanted to escape, why is the affection so lingering that even after six or seven years, it still cannot be completely cut off and forgotten?

Now I speculate on my mood at the time, probably due to the political fanaticism at the time, and I didn't dare to sacrifice my future for love! This was indeed the ambition of the general young people at that time. Naturally, this is also valuable. I have no selfish regret about this at all, but I did let her down. However, looking back at my current wandering and the hardship of life, I feel that she was lucky not to have formed a partnership with me. I cannot make her warm and full, which is the truth. Now she has three children, which is more than enough to comfort her. It is said that life is still okay, which is much better than marrying me.

Contradictory life! I can't love her, and I don't hesitate to return her gifts, but at the same time, I can't forget her.

Amateur Cafe

Modern Unlucky 307

— Wen

Although "September 18th" and "January 28th" have long passed, Puyi's claim to the throne, Japan's northern harassment of Chahar, Xinjiang's independence, and Britain's westward invasion all indicate that the period of national crisis has not yet passed. In this period of national crisis, all Chinese people should endure hardship and strive for self-improvement. However, the general modern men and women do not understand this principle. They eat Western food, wear foreign clothes, talk about love, play golf, go to dance halls, ice skating, and watch movies, living their extravagant and romantic lives as if there is no national crisis. Therefore, people with lofty ideals have risen up in anger, believing that the reason why China is not doing well is the inability of these modern men and women to endure hardship. If all the people in China endured hardship, wouldn't China become rich and strong? Therefore, modern people are unlucky, and everyone attacks them. Last year was the "National Goods Year," and this year is the "Women's National Goods Year." All Chinese people should strive to promote national goods, which is an indisputable principle. However, the general modern men and women have different intentions. They wear American leather shoes, British hats, French clothes, and use Oriental perfume, as if they do not know that they are Chinese. Therefore, people with lofty ideals are angry again, believing that the reason why China's industry and commerce cannot develop is the failure of these modern men and women to use national goods. If they were not like this, wouldn't China's industry and commerce have already developed to the level of Europe and the United States? Therefore, modern people are unlucky, and everyone scolds them.

Writers are the most sensitive and the most able to grasp the times. Since modern men and women have such great sins, and everyone is attacking and scolding them, how can clever writers not use them as the only subject for writing articles? Therefore, articles such as "Modern Girls' Lovers Should Be Shot with Machine Guns," "Modern Wives Sleep with a Dozen Dogs," "Modern Young Masters Skate on Nanjing Road," and "Modern Students Bring Golf Balls to the Lecture Hall" have appeared in batches. Therefore, whether humorous articles, satirical articles, or serious articles, none of them do not talk about modern people. Therefore, modern people are unlucky, and verbal criticism and written attacks are all concentrated on them.

However, modern people say: "There is nothing in the world, and mediocre people disturb themselves! Life is for pleasure, how can we care about so much!"

Biographies of Celebrities

Darwin (II) 308

— Ji Fan

Darwin's university life began in 1825, when he was only sixteen years old. He and his brother entered the University of Edinburgh. His brother was majoring in medicine and was about to complete his studies, while he had just started. During this time, we can also discover his talent.

He was not satisfied with the lectures given at the university at that time. He felt that those professors only said some very boring things, which did not make him get any impression. He once said, "The professor lectured on human anatomy in such a dry and tasteless way, just like himself, that I hated the subject." He also didn't like listening to Duncan's lecture on the properties of rhubarb, and from then on he didn't like the term medicine. But he had a completely different feeling about natural history. When he met MacGillivray, he immediately hit it off. MacGillivray gave him some clam shells, which he regarded as very precious. At the same time, he also informed MacGillivray that he was collecting marine mollusks. From this, it can also be seen that education has a very important role in inspiring students and their interests. How many geniuses like Darwin have been murdered by today's poor education system!

Darwin stayed at the University of Edinburgh for only two years. His family had already found out that he had no intention of becoming a doctor. His father, seeing that Darwin liked hunting, feared that he would become a lazy and do-nothing sportsman in the future, so he advised him to change his major to become a pastor. Although he considered this proposal for a while, he eventually accepted it temporarily; and he accepted the Church of England. During this transition, he had to review classical books, learn Greek, and prepare to go to Cambridge. But he was not a genius for being a pastor after all. When he left Cambridge University to join the Beagle as a naturalist, he couldn't help but smile humorously when he recalled this short period of life. He can only be a scientist.

During Darwin's time at Christ's College, Cambridge, although he had spent some time on mathematics and classics, he was naturally not close to mathematics, and he only perfunctorily dealt with classical theology for the sake of passing the bachelor's exam. Therefore, this period of time cannot but be said to have been completely wasted.

The habit of hunting did not change at this time because of the dogmas of theology. On the contrary, the boredom of lecture hall life forced the genius to wander outdoors. He also learned to ride a horse, often galloping through the fields, indulging in pleasures all day long. And he made friends with all kinds of people with different temperaments, including sports experts, frivolous youths, and young people with lofty ideals. They often took pleasure in drinking, gambling, playing musical instruments, and hunting. And during this period, in addition to recreation, the tendency of genius still appeared, but at that time, ordinary people were often unable to recognize this genius because of the above-mentioned bad impressions.

He was still very eager to collect, and what he was most fascinated by was collecting dung beetles.

In his autobiography, he once described the following interesting story:

"One day, I went to tear off the bark of those old trees again, and found two rare beetles. So I caught one in each hand. Unexpectedly, I later found a third new species. I was reluctant to abandon it, so I put the beetle in my right hand ( ) into my mouth. Ugh! Ugh! This thing is really weird, it actually shot out a very spicy liquid, burning my tongue, I had to spit it out quickly, and as a result, it ran away, and I don't know where the third beetle ran to.

He also loved to scrape off the moss on old trees in winter, or collect parasitic animals attached to the dirt on the bottom of ships, and he often obtained fresh specimens. (To be continued)
